<script>
  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_f254bf44-1760-4678-893b-a15c4f38747d'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };
    if (typeof AppleID !== "undefined") {
      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }
  //]]>
</script>

  <span id="freeText9570633694301177398" style="display:none">Anya Gage has learned that to get anything good in life, you have to work for it. She has no expectations, no dreams. <br /><br />Then she finds herself at a party where she doesn’t want to be and she meets Knight. <br /><br />Knight Sebring knows who he is, what he wants and what he likes. And he gets it. But he never expected something as sweet as Anya Gage to wander into his bedroom during a party he did not expect to be having to borrow his phone. <br /><br />Knight tries to leave Anya to the life she deserves of white picket fences and a man who watches football on Sundays – good, normal and clean. But when Anya comes to his nightclub and finds herself in a situation, he knows someone has to look after her, he can’t fight it anymore and he decides that man will be him. <br /><br />Knight teaches Anya that, just as with the bad, in life you should also expect the good. And he teaches her this by giving it to her. <br /><br />But Knight has a dark past and just as he desires Anya for exactly who she is, he fears when she finds out exactly the man he has become and always intends to be, she’ll leave him for good, normal and clean.</span>

  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794954i/598952._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo 4112e577-7c9e-4de1-8940-375ada644c97_zps06b73044.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>And <b>ANYA</b><br/><a href='http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/d3b48220-5349-4ca0-a7b4-355bcaa830d7_zps2ef563db.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395298i/761328.jpg' alt=' photo d3b48220-5349-4ca0-a7b4-355bcaa830d7_zps2ef563db.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Wars fought over a face like this. A man would work himself into the ground for it, go down to his knees to beg to keep it, endure torture to protect it, take a bullet for it. Poison his brother to possess a face like this.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>Anya first sees Knight at a party. He ma</span>
  <span id="freeText16776712593021532418" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/da5e5665-3185-4931-b5e3-7c6c10558141_zps56f255b2.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379795869i/610883.jpg" alt=" photo da5e5665-3185-4931-b5e3-7c6c10558141_zps56f255b2.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>5 Stars!</b><br><br>Meet <b>KNIGHT</b><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/e3464732-d28c-44a1-a7e4-41b875443ee3_zps75be28ae.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794954i/598951.jpg" alt=" photo e3464732-d28c-44a1-a7e4-41b875443ee3_zps75be28ae.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>“Your Christian name is Knight?” <br>“If that means first name, yeah.”<br> “With a ‘K’”<br> “Yeah, babe, with a ‘K’"<br>“Thats an unusual name.” <br>“Yeah.”<br> “I kind of like it.” <br>“I can die happy.”</i>
</b><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/4112e577-7c9e-4de1-8940-375ada644c97_zps06b73044.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379794954i/598952._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 4112e577-7c9e-4de1-8940-375ada644c97_zps06b73044.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And <b>ANYA</b><br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/d3b48220-5349-4ca0-a7b4-355bcaa830d7_zps2ef563db.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395298i/761328.jpg" alt=" photo d3b48220-5349-4ca0-a7b4-355bcaa830d7_zps2ef563db.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Wars fought over a face like this. A man would work himself into the ground for it, go down to his knees to beg to keep it, endure torture to protect it, take a bullet for it. Poison his brother to possess a face like this.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Anya first sees Knight at a party. He makes quite an impression. He is tall, dark, and handsome. Masculine features, but obviously angry. Anya is at the party with a friend, ready to leave when her cheap phone dies. She goes to a bedroom, which she assumes is Nick’s to use the phone. And there he is. At first Knight is not too happy to see anyone in his room, but he offers to take Anya home. Not really offers, demands is more like it- but thats just Knight's way.<br><br>Knight takes care of Anya from a distance, but one night, she walks into his club. Wearing that dress... and he just couldn’t stay away any longer. Anya is his. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I find all of this very confusing,” I admitted cautiously. <br>“You get in my bed, I’ll sort you out.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Knight is not your normal KA male hero. And I’m more than okay with that! Knight is Possessive. A control freak. A protector. And I love that about him!!!<br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“I have a new boyfriend. He’s awesome. Protective. And scary. And he regularly freaks me out by being all of those at once.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br>He wants Anya. He gets what he wants. <br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“I don’t live in your world. I live in another world. It’s my world. I took it over. I rebuilt it. I own it. I control it. I have a code. Anyone in my world lives by my code.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>When Knight and Anya are together.... It’s HOT! The other KA books I have read did not have sexy times like this! Wow! Knight is super dominate, controlling hero and it carries over to the bedroom. Their chemistry is explosive, and they have an obvious connection. <br><a href="http://s1279.beta.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/d5ec83cd-3e63-4f97-b8ca-adab90e9e429_zps67a398e4.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395298i/761329.jpg" alt=" photo d5ec83cd-3e63-4f97-b8ca-adab90e9e429_zps67a398e4.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><blockquote>
<b>“Uh... you don’t fuck Knight. No way. Knight fucks you.”</b><br><br><b><i>“You gotta know that every second I spend with you it becomes more and more clear you were made for me. A gift I don’t deserve, didn’t earn but I’m not giving back.”</i></b> </blockquote><br>I loved Knight and Anya together. Anya was sweet, independent, and easy to love. She went out of her way to show Knight how much she cared, and do things for him. With his past, having to protect/take care of everyone, it was nice to see. There were some really sweet moments between the two of them...<br><blockquote>
<b><i>“Bottom line, I’m the woman for you, Knight, I was made for you, just as I am. What you don’t get is, you’re the man for me just as you are. I get that honey. And I got it a while ago.”</i></b> <br><br><b><i>“Make a wish, Knight.” His eyes moved, roaming my face, down my body, the cake, more of me then back to my eyes.<br>“Honey, the candles are gonna burn out,” I prompted on a grin.<br>“Let em’” he replied.<br>“Got nothin’ I want. Everything I want is standing right in front of me.”</i></b>
</blockquote><br>As hot as Knight was, he could be really sweet too! He did have his issues, he was rough around the edges, overly possessive and controlling, but he did it out of love. Wanting to take care of her. He was an all around fantastic hero.<br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You love me?”<br> “Baby, you were made for me.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>I know everyone had a big issue with the Daddy/Baby thing... I get it, I do- but it worked for me! I felt that it worked for these characters and their relationship. It intensified the book. <br><br>Overall, this was my kind of book! A KA hero with issues, a sweet and lovable heroine, hot sex scenes, and an interesting story/plot- whats not to love??? Read this unconventional romance with this unfinished hero! I know I’m looking forward to starting the next one asap :D <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/8b491eaf-5fc8-47a0-a965-c35e68743894_zps4bc62424.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395298i/761330.jpg" alt=" photo 8b491eaf-5fc8-47a0-a965-c35e68743894_zps4bc62424.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>First read- 2/2013<br>Fabulous re-read 8/7/13 with two of my besties Lisa Jayne and Anna! Love you girls xoxo<br>Another re-read 3/5/14 for my 28th Birthday &lt;3 <br>Audio re-read 4/2015</span>

<div id="review_308911434" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/308911434" />
    <a title="Jill" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3820197-jill"><img alt="Jill" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1383385041p2/3820197.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/308911434?book_show_action=true">Apr 08, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jill" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jill" href="/user/show/3820197-jill">Jill</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3820197-jill?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer308911434" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1837991760695305730"><br/><b>1.5 stars</b><br/><br/>Perhaps if I'd known from the outset that this would be a story about a hero's need to control the heroine, in and out of the bedroom, I wouldn't have bothered reading this. A man who wants to control and dominate his partner's life is creepy, unstable and unattractive. I can't see the appeal in a man (or woman) dominating their partner. I know that many readers are into bdsm, but if it's not eye-rolling, or boring me to tears, the descriptions are making me laugh. And I'm guessing that</span>
  <span id="freeText1837991760695305730" style="display:none"><br /><b>1.5 stars</b><br /><br />Perhaps if I'd known from the outset that this would be a story about a hero's need to control the heroine, in and out of the bedroom, I wouldn't have bothered reading this. A man who wants to control and dominate his partner's life is creepy, unstable and unattractive. I can't see the appeal in a man (or woman) dominating their partner. I know that many readers are into bdsm, but if it's not eye-rolling, or boring me to tears, the descriptions are making me laugh. And I'm guessing that's not what's supposed to happen. But, total control of a person's life, inside <b>and</b> outside the bedroom? <br /><br />From the blurb and the build-up to this book, I thought I was going to get the baddest, hottest, toughest, giving-the-middle-finger-to-society naughty boy <b>EVER</b>. Perhaps a Tate or Ty on steroids. Instead I got a bloke who biggest claim to badass-ness was his dominance in the bedroom and his control outside of it. Yet if it was only this I had to complain about, and the rest of the story shone, I'd still be a happy little reader. But there was so much here that disappointed me.<br /><br />Things that I didn't like:<br /><br />1) The hero <b>smokes</b>!! What is this, the 60s, the 70s?? A habit like that is about as attractive as a nose-picking. Except the nose-picking is healthier.<br /><br />Some other minor things. The hero is a slut. No, truly a real, live slut. And he wears a black turtleneck, which I guess makes sense as it suits the 70s-era cigarette smoking. Also, he should take lessons from Ty and not talk so much during sex.<br /><br />2) The insta-love/lust of the hero. With just one surreptitious glance at Anya as he walks into a room, he's smitten.<br /><br />3) The <b>nickname</b>. It wouldn't be a Kristen Ashley book without a nickname. This one was <b>Daddy</b>. Enough said.<br /><br />4) The heroine is all legs, tits, ass, and big hair. I’ve only read maybe eight or nine Kristen Ashley books but in each and every one of them we have the same heroine. Physically. I get that it's nice to have women who are shapely, but it’s also nice to mix things up a bit. Can we please have a heroine who is short or I'll settle for medium height. Perhaps one with small breasts. Or one who's boy-shaped (there are women like that) with small ass and hips.<br /><br />5) There was very little romance. Besides the fact, Anya looked good, I never got why Knight fell for her. Or what he saw in her to validate the insta-love.<br /><br />6) Knight's profession.<br /><br />I have loved Kristen Ashley's books. Despite the lack of polish and editing and punctuation, the long-running sentences, the sometimes inane girlie-babble from the heroine, the grunting retorts from the hero, they are entertaining stories. However, this one was just boring. <br /><br />So keen it seems to give us a oh-so-bad hero and to raise the titillation factor with plenty of sex scenes, she forgot a few of the fundamental rules of good writing. Plot and characterisation. I can live with Ms Ashley's different writing style. But a novel without the basics of plot or characterisation is lifeless. <br /><br />The other basic requirement in a romance is....romance. Certainly she turned the heat up with the sex scenes. But I want a story, and oh yeah, a <b>romance</b> that will showcase the love scenes. I want to feel that the hero and heroine will live happily-ever-after. Not likely in this story. For me more sex doesn’t equate to a better story. Sometimes less is more. <br /><br />For someone who's a fan of Kristen Ashley, to see her write this is just a disappointment. I have to emphasise it wasn’t really my dislike of the hotter sex scenes that lowered the rating for me, but rather I didn’t get what I was promised. A good romance with a badboy hero. I wanted a badboy, and I got a dickhead. I want <b>BAD</b>, not nuts! <br /><br />But mostly I want a story, a real story with great plot, interesting characterisations, a to-die-for romance. Sure I got plenty of hot and heavy sex. But at the expense of an entertaining story and wonderful romance told in that unputdownable style unique to Kristen Ashley. This was no <i>Sweet Dreams</i> or <i>Lady Luck</i> or <i>Law Man</i> or....<br /><br />Although this was a major disappointment - and I do hope that this type of hero is not going to be the focus of her future writing - Kristen Ashley is still to my mind a great story-teller. <i>Knight</i> simply does not showcase her talent.<br /><br /><b>Steam:</b> 3.5-4<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="1837991760695305730" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_443232064" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/443232064" />
    <a title="Dd" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9444787-dd"><img alt="Dd" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/f_50x66-6a03a5c12233c941481992b82eea8d23.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/443232064?book_show_action=true">Oct 27, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dd" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dd" href="/user/show/9444787-dd">Dd</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer443232064" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer550801539227700532"><br/><b>Oh.<br/>My.<br/>God.<br/><br/>Hello Readers.<br/><br/>Call me crazy but I really liked this book.</b><br/><br/><i>I mean how many times have you dreamed of a white knight coming to sweep you off your feet??<br/><br/>Slay down dragons for you??</i><br/><br/><b>Hmmm...A knight of my own....what I wouldn't do for one!!</b><br/><br/>But errrr...there's a slight problem!!<br/><br/>Well you see this knight is very,very rough....<br/><br/><b>1)</b>He can't speak a sentence without using the words f*ck or shit.<br/><br/><b>2)</b>He is a control freak.Freak as in real freak.<br/><br/><b>3)</b>His ego is not just the <b>humble size</b> of Texas but whole of </span>
  <span id="freeText550801539227700532" style="display:none"><br /><b>Oh.<br />My.<br />God.<br /><br />Hello Readers.<br /><br />Call me crazy but I really liked this book.</b><br /><br /><i>I mean how many times have you dreamed of a white knight coming to sweep you off your feet??<br /><br />Slay down dragons for you??</i><br /><br /><b>Hmmm...A knight of my own....what I wouldn't do for one!!</b><br /><br />But errrr...there's a slight problem!!<br /><br />Well you see this knight is very,very rough....<br /><br /><b>1)</b>He can't speak a sentence without using the words f*ck or shit.<br /><br /><b>2)</b>He is a control freak.Freak as in real freak.<br /><br /><b>3)</b>His ego is not just the <b>humble size</b> of Texas but whole of North America!!<br /><br /><b>4)</b>And most importantly he has a <b>DADDY COMPLEX</b>!!<br /><br /><br />Now let's meet with his baby,Anya---<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"Wars fought over a face like this," he murmured like he was talking to himself, my heart stopped beating and his thumbs moved lightly across my cheeks. "A man would work himself into the ground for it, go down to his knees to beg to keep it, endure torture to protect it, take a bullet for it," his eyes came to mine, "poison his brother to possess a face like this."</i>
</b><br /><br /><br />It all starts with a party....<br /><br />But before that let me introduce the one who plays the most important role in the story-- A cheap mobile phone.<br /><br />Oh no,I'm not kidding with you.If this <b>CHEAP</b> phone was not there,they would never have met.<br /><br /><br /><b>As I was telling you,it all starts with a party.....</b><br /><br /><br />Anya was standing in the corner.She did not want to be there.But her friend Sandrine,who's a gold digger,did not want to miss a party thrown by Nick Sebring and dragged her along.<br /><br />There she saw him for the first time.He was very tall,very handsome and very angry.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"I was a woman and he was the kind of man a woman would look at.Any woman."</i>
</b><br /><br /><br />But he was gone the next moment.Taking this as a cue,she had to leave alone when Sandrine refused to leave.So she got her coat and was just going to call for a taxi with <b>that cheap phone</b>,when her battery ran out.But there was a phone inside a bedroom which she assumed to be Nick's.She went in and was just going to call for a taxi when she heard a low,smooth,very deep,definitely annoyed man's voice asking,<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"What the fuck?"</i>
</b><br /><br /><i>So,now do you see Readers,why that cheap phone plays the most essential part?</i><br /><br />Knight ended up taking her home.He wouldn't take no for an answer.And that marked their beginning---<br /><br /><b>
  <i>"Um, I don't know your name but -"<br />"Knight,"he stated,cutting me off.<br />"Right, Mr. Knight - "<br />"No, Knight,"he interrupted me again...<br />"Thats what I said, Knight," I told him. "Now, Mr. Knight -"<br />"No, not Mr. Knight. Knight. My name is Knight."<br />"Your Christian name is Knight?"<br />"If that means first name,yeah."<br />"With a K?"...<br />"Yeah, babe, with a 'K'."</i>
</b><br /><br />Knight tried to stay away from Anya after that.Though,he made sure that the building she lived in got secured and gave her a brand new,certainly-not-cheap phone,which Anya tried to return.<br /><br />But all that changed when she arrived at his club and Nick tried to get her alone.<br /><br /><b>This time he claimed her.<br /><br /><i>"What...the fuck...is the matter with you?"he asked slowly,his voice still vibrating,the fury still radiating.<br />"I didn't do anything!" <br />"You put on that dress, didn't you?"he whispered and it was sinister.<br />"What?"I whispered back.<br />"You...do not...leave your house...dressed like that...without being on the arm of a man like me," he ground out.<br />"A man like you?" I whispered.<br />"A man who'd shoot another man in the face if he even looked at you. Yeah,Anya,a man...like...me"</i><br /><br />And thus he owned her.Body.Heart.And Soul.</b><br /><br />---------------------------------------------------------------------<br /><br /><b>WARNING</b>--This is an unconventional LOVE story.If you are afraid that you won't be getting a hero,then let me assure you,you'll get a hero for sure.<br /><br />Dark?Egotistical?Crazy?Control freak....yes he is all that.<br /><br />But he never hurt Anya or anyone else just for the sake of hurting.<br /><b>His simple rule-You get as good you give!!</b><br /><br /><b>
  <i>"It’s all I know Anya. Protection. I was born then I was raised to be a shield." </i>
</b><br /><br /><br /><i>The ending will leave you with a warm,fuzzy feeling!!!**sigh**<br /><br />Just remember,there's someone made for everyone.And Anya was made for Knight.And they fit together perfectly.<br /><br /><br />That's all for now...<br /><br /><b>Ta-Ta!!</b><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /><br /> <br /><br /><br /><br /></i></span>
  <a data-text-id="550801539227700532" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer303278794" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16256674154774057170"><b>
  <u>5 stars</u>
</b><br/><br/> I can understand why this book did not work for everyone! I, however, loved reading every page of this story. <br/><br/>Kristen Ashley gave me what I wanted. She gave me a <b>true</b> anti-hero–one who would challenge what I consider acceptable behavior in my hero. Knight was the type of character who generated, for me, an inner turmoil between my desire for a hero who genuinely loves his heroine (which he did) and my knowledge that he had few, if any, redeeming qualities, and frankly, didn't deserve</span>
  <span id="freeText16256674154774057170" style="display:none"><b>
  <u>5 stars</u>
</b><br /><br /> I can understand why this book did not work for everyone! I, however, loved reading every page of this story. <br /><br />Kristen Ashley gave me what I wanted. She gave me a <b>true</b> anti-hero–one who would challenge what I consider acceptable behavior in my hero. Knight was the type of character who generated, for me, an inner turmoil between my desire for a hero who genuinely loves his heroine (which he did) and my knowledge that he had few, if any, redeeming qualities, and frankly, didn't deserve that heroine.<br /><br />I could never accept a man like Knight in real life; however, Knight is a fantasy, and, for me, I could look past all his imperfections and fall in love with the love story. If you can do the same, then you will enjoy this story. If you can't, this book probably is not for you. <br /><br /><i>If you're already a Kristen Ashley addict, or interested in checking out her books, be sure to stop by our <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/66492.Kristen_Ashley_Addict_s_Support_Group" rel="nofollow noopener">Kristen Ashley Addict's Support Group</a> here on Goodreads!</i></span>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer303206728" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer7812065683869311757">1 Star<br/><br/><i>First, an apology. It is not my intent to *bash* this author. She has provided me MANY hours of enjoyment and many characters to love.</i><br/><br/>I'm conflicted. I did like some things, but it was inconsistent. To say I liked the characters, I did, but then I sincerely didn't like some of the characterizations. Maybe you can help me out..?<br/><br/>To be fair, I'm not a normal BDSM reader, but this was what I'd call BDSM light. It wasn't over the top, so I could hang.<br/><br/>What did I have issues with?<br/>1 -- The whole B</span>
  <span id="freeText7812065683869311757" style="display:none">1 Star<br /><br /><i>First, an apology. It is not my intent to *bash* this author. She has provided me MANY hours of enjoyment and many characters to love.</i><br /><br />I'm conflicted. I did like some things, but it was inconsistent. To say I liked the characters, I did, but then I sincerely didn't like some of the characterizations. Maybe you can help me out..?<br /><br />To be fair, I'm not a normal BDSM reader, but this was what I'd call BDSM light. It wasn't over the top, so I could hang.<br /><br />What did I have issues with?<br />1 -- The whole Baby/Daddy thing. I didn't mind Knight calling Anya baby - an endearment I can handle. I could even buy Anya calling Knight Daddy .. maybe. We all know those sweet little southern ladies who call their husbands Daddy, so okay. Plus, this didn't happen until about 40% of the way through the book, so maybe .. but then during sex. And the insistence of this by Knight and just YUCK!! WTF! I'm mean this was just F**KING WHACKED!! To the point it turned my stomach. The whole book could have done without this. Seriously whacked.<br />2 -- Ever heard the phrase "some people can justify murder"? Knight has a "stable" of 57 women - prostitutes. He explains this because his mother was a prostitute before meeting "Carl". She had it rough. So, he can take care of these girls, provide protection for a small price, not take "trade" from them. Providin' a service you know. He takes care of these woman. Oldest trade and it will always be around ... blah, blah, blah. WTF!! Seriously, Anya appreciates him taking care of these women and he keeps this separate from her so all good .. right? WHACKED again!<br />3 -- His absolute rudeness to her in the "name of control". <b>Anya. Here. Now.</b> Go. F**k. Yourself. I say. And she is so, "I love this man". WTF!! I really hope readers reading this realize this sort of rudeness is unacceptable. They don't assume because this is written into a book, by an author they love ... Rudeness in any form or fashion is unacceptable. A total lack of respect. Period.<br /><br />I bought this book the day/hour it was out. Watching all the back and forth by the other KA fans. This has been my pattern for this authors books. I think I may be a bit more careful in the future.<br /><br />I did like these characters, until I didn't. I did like this story, until I didn't. I hated how at the very end she threw some sweetness in, when there is no way this can end sweetly.. this guy is still a pimp. He did lose a bit of the rude [see I want to like him..]. I really don't care what these two do in the bedroom; two consenting adults .. blah. And it seriously wasn't bad. What I do mind is the whole "Daddy" thing. Made me feel a voyeur at an incest waiting to happen. Oh, guess what? The sweetness at the end? Was a sweet little baby girl laying in "Daddy's" arms. Sick much?<br /><br />Remember, this is only my opinion. I do appreciate the author "branching" out into erotica [this would be erotica light]. I appreciate her talent and her need to explore. But, for this reader, there was a boundary crossed, that I seriously hadn't thought would ever be an issue for me reading KA. What a HUGE surprise - me. <br /><br />I got the uggys.<br /><br />Read at your own risk.<br /> </span>

<div id="review_488972701" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/488972701" />
    <a title="• Lisa •" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa"><img alt="• Lisa •" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1576172089p2/11963959.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/488972701?book_show_action=true">Dec 29, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="• Lisa •" class="user" itemprop="url" name="• Lisa •" href="/user/show/11963959-lisa">• Lisa •</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/11963959-lisa?shelf=love-you-forever-and-ever">love-you-forever-and-ever</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer488972701" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12120726742727603565"><b>FIVE 'THE DADDY' STARS</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>“You don't need to like me to let me fuck you but since I like you, I'd prefer it that way.” </i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394046015i/8800476._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>CAUTION</b> a word of warning, do not proceed with this book if you are offended by any kind of over domineering, deliciously tempting alpha characters. This book would more than likely not be for you, however luckily for me I love, love, loved every page and gladly spent my time with this dangerous hero. 'Knight' is the kind of book that puts yourself in an anxious state waiting fo</span>
  <span id="freeText12120726742727603565" style="display:none"><b>FIVE 'THE DADDY' STARS</b><br><br><b>
  <i>“You don't need to like me to let me fuck you but since I like you, I'd prefer it that way.” </i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394046015i/8800476._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>CAUTION</b> a word of warning, do not proceed with this book if you are offended by any kind of over domineering, deliciously tempting alpha characters. This book would more than likely not be for you, however luckily for me I love, love, loved every page and gladly spent my time with this dangerous hero. 'Knight' is the kind of book that puts yourself in an anxious state waiting for your next spare time to read. For my reading tastes there was nothing not to love, this Novel is a lively eye opener and fabulously entertaining read. I've now crowned Kristen Ashley as my fairy-book-godmother as I'm sure she waved her literary magic Wand over me as I was reading this book. This story boasts my favourite 'book husband' to date and is most confidently one of my most treasured alpha stories, here are the rest of my 'I love the daddy' book thoughts ...<br><br><b>What's it all about?</b><br>Knight Sebring is a tall, brooding, strong, dangerous but overprotective and devilishly handsome business man. He is ruthless with all his endeavours and stops at nothing to get what he wants out of life. When Anya Gage walks into his life a relationship of epic proportions ensues where the test of time and love is battled out between two hearts. Secrets, shock reveals and uncertainty mean this love is challenged at every turn but this alpha is determined to make this love his forever.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394051641i/8801468._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>What did I love?</b><br>I've already sat at the book confessional and declared this book as a favourite of mine, so here are some of the reasons why; 'Knight' is full of Tantalisingly good chapter titles, which are bursting with great story telling and descriptive scenes. Kristen Ashley provides her readers with male characters to die for and Knight is no exception, be prepared to be shocked and fall in love, Mr Sebring is not a character to be missed, with every amazing male we hope to find an equally loveable heroine to fall in love with and I believe that the author delivered just that in this story. I found the relationship between the pair refreshingly original and believable. I can't deny that I love a well rounded story of a bad boy and good girl falling helplessly in love and Kristen Ashley showcases that perfectly here. I don't think I'll ever tire of this genre of book, if authors continue to write them, i'll read them. Knight Sebring's name should be next to the dictionary definition of swoon, he is undoubtedly a love him or loathe him character, he won't be hitting everyone's favourite lists but he's certainly on the top of my Christmas wish list this year. This couple are now a firm favourite of mine, I loved the chemistry and connection that Kristen ashley created right from chapter one and I want everyone to fall in love with this story right alongside me.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394051641i/8801469._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Final thoughts ...</b><br>This book was all kinds of right and all of the best kinds of wrong, I could not get enough of this story, and felt a tad bereft when I turned that final page. Life can be messy, hurtful, hard, heartbreaking, love isn't always perfect, people make mistakes and wrong choices, 'Knight' wraps all of above up in one gorgeously addictive story and shows that ultimately when two people are meant to be - it just works. 'Knight' was my first book by Kristen Ashley and I'm 100% sure it will not be my last, her writing style had me hooked. A stunning beginning, an entertaining middle and an epilogue that was the icing on the cake. You would be crazy to miss out, go grab it readers ... Kisses. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1394052416i/8801589._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>*Originally devoured in January, taken for another 'spin' as a re-read with the girls in August 2013, now read for the third time March 2014.*</i>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="12120726742727603565" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

She heads to the nearest bedroom to find a land line, so she can call a cab.<br><br>If you would prefer Anya to call a cab and go home by herself, click here : <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Sorry, you're out of luck. Please stop reading romance novels altogether. Your adventure has ended. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>If you would prefer Anya to meet a tall, handsome, pissed off man who offers her a ride home, click here : <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Your wish has been granted. Please continue reading. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>This new stranger, only known as "Knight," shows an interest in Anya. We enter a place in the book I'd like to call : <b>I can't believe it's not <s>butter</s> Fifty.</b><br><br>If you enjoyed the book Fifty Shades of Grey click here : <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[This book should be your thing. Please continue reading. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>If you hated the book Fifty Shades of Grey because of Ana, click here : <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[You might still enjoy this book. Other than one very brief "squee" dance inside of this woman's head, there are no inner goddesses in sight. Please continue reading. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>If you hated the book Fifty Shades of Grey because of Christian's possessiveness, click here :<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[You may possibly be out of luck. While Knight gets extra points for dirty talk, awesome sexorzing and all-around badassness, he still has a few Christian similarities. Note the faded jeans, suits during business hours, effed up mom issues, as well as the need to control finances (including gifting a car) and provide security for his woman. The men are not clones but if you are not a fan of controlling alphas in any sense, this is not the book for you. Your adventure ends here. If you can handle some alpha behavior and don't mind your man possibly threatening and/or ass kicking those who mess with you, then you may continue reading. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>If you hated the book Fifty Shades of Grey because Christian had psychological issues, click here :<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[You're in luck! Knight seems to be fairly stable. He enjoys being touched and doesn't mind mixing it up in the bedroom without having to be asked. This man is, quite literally, THE man in the bedroom. Rough sex? - check. Gentle lovemaking? - check. Cuddling? - check. Where Fifty had a few chemistry issues, Knight scored big points on this front. You may continue reading. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Knight and Anya hit it off. Each of them fear the other is keeping secrets, so they both try to investigate in order to find out what's going on behind the scenes. However, after Anya starts to ask questions she's told by Knight to stop, so she does. Yet...Knight doesn't seem to stop digging. I wasn't crazy about this part of the story. Even though there was no contract, she accepted demands with hardly any question. Knight took some of his actions (snooping, hovering, demanding she be at places at set times) to a place that could possibly freak most women out.<br><br>Even though I'm making a note that the above behavior doesn't do it for me...I'm going to disclaimer that we are working with a romance that imo straddles the realm of mainstream contemporary and BDSM erotica. Different genre = different rules. People often read erotica to have their kinky itches scratched. Some people love the D/s system outside of the bedroom and might find Knight to be their perfect book hero. I prefer my D/s to be sexual ONLY, with the relationship outside of the bedroom conducted as equal partners in every aspect. Anyway, there's your warning, so you know what you're getting into. <br><br>Our couple develops a very close and loving relationship - suprised? I was. As mentioned earlier, Knight may be dominant but he <i>adores</i> his Anya. The high point of this book was the way he worshipped his woman. I am also awarding Knight a highly coveted "Dirty Talker" award. I thought Flynn from Willing Victim had it going on, but that man has just been dethroned. If nothing else, I would read the book if you love a man who can talk about what he loves while he's giving it to you. This man is on fire!!! He had me at, "want to own your body and beauty," and whatever else he was saying in the bedroom as I was in my giddy female reading state. Yes, please.<br><br>On to the "terms of endearment."<br><br>Do you like the use of such terms as baby, daddy, etc.? <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Uh...I guess you're in luck? You may continue reading. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>Do you hate the aforementioned terms? <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I do too. So, so much. HUGE point deduction for this. There's also other cringe-worthy terms such as "womb clenching." If amazing sexy talk would offset this hatred, please continue reading. If no amount of epic sexy talk would make up for the constant and cringe-worthy use of ridiculous "sugar daddy" lingo, then your journey ends here. I understand. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Other random points :<br><br>Are you okay with a bad boy who might in fact do bad things when it comes to business or skirting the law? If yes : <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[You'll be fine. You may continue reading <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>If the answer is no : <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Outta luck. Really, why are you still here in this review? You should have left by now. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>The ending...<br><br>Do you want a happy ever after? (HEA) If yes : <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Tada! Wish granted. It's a bit of a given though, right? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br>Don't care? <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[It's romance. Are you surprised? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>.<br><br><br><b>Final analysis :</b><br><br>This was my first KA book. Apparently, I picked one of the wilder ones to start with, as this is less mainstream than some of her other works. I will be trying out one of her more "mainstream" books to see how I like her other work. <br><br>My opinion :<br><br>Pros - Great bedroom domination, man who is a loving caregiver, sexual variety and epic dirty talk.<br>Cons - A man who wanted to control too much of the woman's personal life outside of the bedroom, which is so not my thing. Also, I was a bit confused by this woman who had a spine in some areas yet accepted things without question in others, which was sort of a contradiction. I think it was explained that she found out being a sub sort of turned her crank, and if so, this probably shouldn't bother me...but it kind of does.<br></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

<div id="review_421318121" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/421318121" />

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/421318121?book_show_action=true">Sep 24, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Aestas Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Aestas Book Blog" href="/user/show/5604583-aestas-book-blog">Aestas Book Blog</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer421318121" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2172767899645063491"><b> 4 stars. 5 stars. 2 stars. 1 star.... I guess that makes 3? It doesn't feel right to give it 3, but that kind of is the middle ground of my feelings. </b><br/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392288i/755245._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>If you like <b> controlling </b> men, this is the book for you!! If not, you may wish to stay away... <br/><br/>This is the darker side of KA! <b> In case you have not read any of her books before, you should know that most of them are NOT like this. Pleeease dont judge her books based on this one!! </b> <br/><br/>I'd been putting this book off for a while because I knew there wer</span>
  <span id="freeText2172767899645063491" style="display:none"><b> 4 stars. 5 stars. 2 stars. 1 star.... I guess that makes 3? It doesn't feel right to give it 3, but that kind of is the middle ground of my feelings. </b><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392288i/755245._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>If you like <b> controlling </b> men, this is the book for you!! If not, you may wish to stay away... <br><br>This is the darker side of KA! <b> In case you have not read any of her books before, you should know that most of them are NOT like this. Pleeease dont judge her books based on this one!! </b> <br><br>I'd been putting this book off for a while because I knew there were a lot of controversial things in it that I was really worried I wouldn't be okay with them. And in the end, as much as it hurts my heart to say it, I wasn't okay with them.... but, and here's the weird thing... I actually still really liked the story. Despite hating certain parts of it. I know that's weird, but there's nothing I can do about it.<br><br>Beware. This book makes me a little ranty... consider yourselves warned :P<br><br><i> "Um, I don't know your name but -"<br>"Knight,"...<br>"Right, Mr. Knight - "<br>"No, Knight," ...<br>"Thats what I said, Knight," I told him. "Now, Mr. Knight -"<br>He...turned his eyes to me...<br>"No, not Mr. Knight. Knight. My name is Knight." ...<br>"With a K?"...<br>"Yeah, babe, with a 'K'."...<br>That's an unusual name."...<br>"Yeah," he agreed...<br>"I kinda like it," ...<br>"I can die happy" </i><br><br>When Anya stumbles into Knight's bedroom one night at a party she doesn't want to be at and that he doesn't even want in his house, he informs her that he's going to take her home. No questions. He's unlike anyone she's ever met - pissed, scary, bossy, controlling, insanely sexy, yet utterly protective and caring. Days later she can't get him out of her head. He's in her dreams, her thoughts, her mind... In many ways, they are polar opposites, in many ways they are perfect for each other, but either way, they are both unquestionably drawn to each other and so begins their unconventional romance.<br><br>As terrifyingly scary controlling as Knight came off as first, I actually, oddly enough, kinda fell instantly love with him. He radiated protectiveness. I loved that about him. And when he told her she should feel safe with him, I totally believed him. I felt safe with him, which is weird, I know considering I'm the reader, but you get what I mean...<br><br><i> "What...the fuck... is the matter with you?" ...<br>What? ...<br>"I didn't do anything!" ...<br>"You put on that dress, didn't you?"...<br>"What?"...<br>"You... do not... leave your house... dressed like that... without being on the arm of a man like me," he ground out...<br>"A man like you?" I whispered back.<br>"A man who'd shoot another man in the face he even looked at you. Yeah, Anya, a man... like... me" </i><br><br>**SHIVERS**<br><br>Everything about Knight screamed opulence, power, <b> control </b>. He was such an oxymoron of a character. Both a gentleman and a jerk. Rough and yet never cruel. He was no knight in shining armor. More like a dark, scary knight. But one that <b> you knew without a doubt would go to the ends of the world and back to keep harm from those he loved. </b> He was a bossy, <i> <b> seriously </b></i> controlling , sophisticated Alpha caveman. He knew who he was and what he wanted and wasn't going to play games to get them.<br><br>Throughout the whole book, even throughout all my issues (about which I will go into detail in a moment), I never, ever, not even once, doubted that his heart was in the right place. He was an anti-hero. Gorgeous. Flawed. Protective. Fuckhot. <b> Dominant. </b> Truly an "unfinished hero".<br><br><i> <b> “It’s all I know Anya. Protection. I was born then I was raised to be a shield." </b> </i><br><br>Just like with his dialogue (which I loved, by the way), everything about him was clipped, efficient, and yet strangely heart warming.<br><br><i> <b> "Wars fought over a face like this," he murmured... "A man would work himself into the ground for it, go down to his knees to beg to keep it, endure torture to protect it, take a bullet for it..."<br>Oh.<br>My.<br>God. <br>"Knight," I breathed.<br>"You are not walkin' away from me." </b></i> <br><br>Anya, I loved. She was independent, took care of herself, was very down-to-earth and appreciated the little things in life. I loved that despite her tragic back-story, she didn't let that consume her life and had found a way to move on positively.... I think that, in the end, Knight could have learned a bit from her.<br><br>Its weird but I was kind of bracing myself going into this book... I knew about the "Daddy" thing (I'll go into more detail in a second) and I was honestly almost preparing myself not to like Knight and had all my defensive shields up ready to kind of hate him, but I honestly couldn't stop myself from totally falling head over heels in love with him. Especially in the first half of the book, he made me tingle...<br><br>The hotness between them was explosive!! Their chemistry was strong, but very subtle. No in-your-face instant declarations of love, but it didn't mean you couldn't absolutely FEEL their connection and what they felt for each other.<br><br>I was in 5 star LOVE with the story until the 40% mark... then things started to get difficult for me and really pushed the limits of my comfort zone. I loved Knight's character and I kept trying to breathe deeply and not be judgmental but by 42%, I was <b> NOT okay </b> with the things he was saying.<br><br>I'll admit, up till that point, I was wondering what all the fuss about this book was about but at that point I was STRONGLY feeling the need to dash my Kindle against the wall and put the book down. He was just WAY too over-the-top controlling. I kept fighting to stay in love with him and just had to remove myself from the story a little.<br><br>I took a breather for a few hours and then dove back it. I had fallen in love with his character enough that I wanted to know why he was the way he was. And he promised that he'd tell so I stuck with the story... I was having this extreme love/hate relationship with him and was totally sympathizing how Anya was feeling:<br><br><i> "You scare me, confuse me, freak me out and you're also sweet so I don't know what to do with you." ....<br>"You get in my bed, I'll sort you out." </i><br><br>I'll lay it out. He's into punishments. Not random cruelty, but if she does something he doesn't like, he spanks her with his hand or strap. Personally, I'm <i> reallllly </i> not into that. Big turn off for me despite the fact that I can admit that scenes where they are written can be really hot but its the concept of them that rubs me way the fucking wrong way. Like WAAAAY wrong. But I had to realize that it wasn't about whether or not I liked it. Clearly Anya did, so again... I just tried to open my mind and accept it. She was happy. He was happy... ok.<br><br>With him, it wasn't about kink. It was purely about control. His back story does come out later to explain it but I was still thanking God for small favors when I read this: <i> "I am not into kink, animals, candle wax... knives, blood, needles, clamps, strangulation, and definitely not any shit that goes beyond that." </i> *WHEW* Good to know! ... (I'm sorry, animals???? That was even an ﻿option?? ﻿ok, I'm getting side tracked... back to the review)<br><br>The depth of their feeling for each other was beautiful but during those punishment scenes, I felt like there was a wall between me and the story because even though I was trying hard not to judge, some of the stuff just was just so not appealing to me that it kept me a little removed even though I really cared for the story. Gah! That sounds weird even to me!<br><br>So I kinda fought my feeling about him... I'd get into a point where I thought I could be okay with everything, but then he'd do or say something that would literally make me cringe away from my kindle in disgust..... <i> "Who owns you?" </i> really? REALLY??? OWNS?? ok... trying to remind myself that Anya likes it :| *deep breath*<br><br>And lets not forget the big elephant in the room regarding this book: <br><b> The "Daddy" issue. </b><br>For those of you who don't know, I'll lay it out. In the bedroom, he calls her "my baby" (which on its own is sweet), but he also has her call him "Daddy".... the combination of the two was NOT. OKAY. with me. <br>I never got over my issue with it. <b> I cringed <i> every </i> time I read it. </b> I'm sorry to say that it really creeped me way-the-freaking-hell out. It just felt so WRONG. I'm sorry, I try my best not be judgmental in life, but it just made me want to gag, vomit and put the book down.<br><br>It was just too much for me. Example: <br><i> "My baby wants her Daddy." </i> Ewwwww *shudders* WHY?? Ugh. <br><i> "Ride your Daddy." "Yes, Daddy."</i> Nononono!!! God. YUK!! <br>Here's another <i> <b> "hold onto Daddy's cock". </b></i>  I'm sorry, but that made me physically ill. I don't even want to THINK about those two words in the same sentence. EVER. Fucking gross.... I just kept trying to remind myself of how sweet he was when he wasn't calling himself her Daddy. I loved his character, I really did. He was so sweet and Alpha and adored her but still...just EWWWWW!!<br><br>And let it be clarified... it wasn't the Daddy thing alone that bothered me. I could have probably gotten used to that. It was the fact that it was combined with "my baby". Its kind of <i> impossible </i> for me to read that and not have my mind go to places it really did NOT want to go.<br><br>Slight spoiler in regards to the Daddy thing but VERY important regarding the most important reason why I wasn't okay with it : <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ I didn't like the Daddy thing, but I was dealing with it because it was just their 'thing' ... BUT, then, it was written in the epilogue that <b> their daughter was curled up on her "Daddy's" chest.<i> WHAT. THE. FUCK ?!? </i> </b> I spent the book trying to square myself with the idea that, to them, Daddy didn't mean father and was a term of endearment... So I figured that for sure if they had kids, he would always be Dad, not Daddy, so WHY WAS IT USED IN THAT CONTEXT????? Arrrgh, that, I cannot square myself with. Ewwww. Gag. Barf.  <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>But the thing was that Knight was not an ass. God, his moments of sweet and loving warmed my heart every time right up to the point where I pretty much would forget all my issues with him. He cared for and loved Anya SO deeply. I just had to accept that his way of showing it and his world were different. Seriously, when he wasn't grossing me out, I really, really loved him!!<br><br><i> <b> "I love you, Anya, you're the only woman who's had that from me and you're the only one who ever will." </b> </i><br><br>Interestingly, there is no 90% freakout moment in this, like with most KA books. Instead, there is a big revelation about Knight that comes out, and I know it was pretty controversial, but oddly enough I was totally fine with it. He explained the reason behind it and that was good enough of an explanation for me to totally accept it.<br><br><b> A lot of things about Knight made me want to gag, cringe, and shudder... but a lot of things about him made me melt, warmed my heart and had me fanning myself... And I really LOVED both Knight and Anya's characters for a whole number of reasons and despite my occasional gagging, it was a really good book. I don't know if that makes any sense, but its the truth. Knight and Anya were undeniably perfect for each other. They completed each other, found peace in each other, and loved each other with all their hearts. That part was beautiful. And, at the end of the day, that's what matters most, right? </b><br><br>I had a few issues with how the book ended and where Knight ended up as a character. I guess he really was an Unfinished Hero in the end. One who cared strongly, deeply and undeniably for what was his. But I wished he's have changed just a bit more. You know, sometimes change is growth. And just because a person is the way they are, doesn't mean a little improvement would be a bad thing and it doens't mean they are giving up who they are. I think that's a lesson he would have done well to take to heart. <br><br><b> **SLIGHT SPOILER ALERT IF YOU READ ON** </b><br><br>1) It was written in the epilogue that their daughter was curled up on her "Daddy's" chest. WHAT. THE. FUCK ?!? I spent the book trying to square myself with the idea that, to them, Daddy didn't mean father and was a term of endearment... So I figured that for sure if they had kids, he would always be Dad, not Daddy, so WHY WAS IT USED IN THAT CONTEXT????? Arrrgh, that, I cannot square myself with. Ewwww. Gag. Barf.<br><br>2) I didn't like how he never accepted celebrating Christmas. I understand why he is the way he is as a person. It makes sense... But I wished he'd had changed more. He was just too rigidly set in his ways. No Christmas??? C'mon. WTF? I'm not Christian and even I celebrate Christmas - tree, presents, music, food and all. It's a beautiful holiday, a time to be with family, share love, make memories. I think it would have made him grow a lot as a person if he could have learned to appreciate that. And what about his kids?? Was he planning on being the Grinch for eternity?? grrrrrrr<br>**EDIT: okay, so someone told me that apparently, on a thread somewhere, KA said that Knight would actually celebrate Christmas with his kids. Ok. That's amazing, and I'm very happy he would have gotten to that point. BUT, I'd have wished he'd gotten to that point in the epilogue somewhere so we could have seen his character growth. Cuz without knowing that, it didn't make me look too favorably on him in that respect and not everyone would know about that little comments made on a thread somewhere.<br><br>Oh, Knight... I want to love you. I DO love you. You just make it so hard at times...<br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392288i/755246._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380392288i/755247.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer307204703" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer5545820536038743562">5 stars – Contemporary Erotic Romance<br/><br/>This is Kristen Ashley’s first venture into the “erotic” romance genre, and I <i>loved</i> it! Knight Sebring is a seriously sexy, magnetic, dark anti-hero and all kinds of yummy “Dom”ineering alpha hotness. Anya Gage is very likeable and genuine and one of my favorite KA heroines. I really enjoyed their captivating, intense connection, dynamic relationship, emotional progression, and explosive bedroom scenes! YOWZA!<br/> <br/>Ms. Ashley took a gamble with this, and I imagine</span>
  <span id="freeText5545820536038743562" style="display:none">5 stars – Contemporary Erotic Romance<br><br>This is Kristen Ashley’s first venture into the “erotic” romance genre, and I <i>loved</i> it! Knight Sebring is a seriously sexy, magnetic, dark anti-hero and all kinds of yummy “Dom”ineering alpha hotness. Anya Gage is very likeable and genuine and one of my favorite KA heroines. I really enjoyed their captivating, intense connection, dynamic relationship, emotional progression, and explosive bedroom scenes! YOWZA!<br> <br>Ms. Ashley took a gamble with this, and I imagine some readers/fans will be put off by certain aspects, like the BDSM (D/s) elements and Knight’s dark side. He’s definitely an enigmatic, powerful “anti-hero”, but that’s one of the things I loved most about it. And I’ve read quite a bit of erotic and BDSM romances, so for me, this is actually on the somewhat lite/mild side, but it’s still gratifyingly steamy!<br><br>Controversy and Quibbles:<br><br>1) Spank Me Daddy<br><br>Knight had Anya answer/call him “Daddy” instead of “Master” or “Sir” in their sex play, which usually sets off my ick factor alert, but it really didn’t bother me in this. Somehow Knight mastered it, and I actually found this <i>“Daddy”</i> more smokin’ hot than creepy. <i>“Come to/for Daddy?”</i> If/when it’s Knight Sebring demanding it? <i>Oh Hell Yeah!</i> <br><br>2) I’m No Mr. Nice Guy...aka...Knight’s Big Secret<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Knight is a pimp. WTF?!?! But hey, he treats his stable of women much better than his smarmy predecessor and he once covered Anya with a blanket while she was napping, so it’s okay. <i>*dramatic eye roll*</i> It just didn’t seem right to me that he would continue to profit from the world’s oldest profession, despite his reasoning and assurances that his girls are well treated and protected, especially considering his mother’s tragic past as a prostitute and how it impacted him when he was a little boy. And not to mention the fact that he’s already filthy rich. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>3) HEA But Knight Isn’t Traditional<br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Knight wouldn’t “officially” marry Anya or give her his last name because it’s just not him (too white picket fence and traditional). Yet he gave her a ring and very reception-like party and was excited and enthusiastic about having kids. Hmmm...isn’t that a bit ironic? <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br><br>Overall, I’m a very satisfied Kristen Ashley fangirl and sincerely hope she pens more erotic romances! 5 stars! <br><br>Favorite Knight quotes:<br><br><i>“Wars fought over a face like this,” he murmured like he was talking to himself, my heart stopped beating and his thumbs moved lightly across my cheeks. “A man would work himself into the ground for it, go down to his knees to beg to keep it, endure torture to protect it, take a bullet for it,” his eyes came to mine, “poison his brother to possess a face like this.”<br><br>“And I wake up happy, baby, because I possess beauty and I own that beauty in all the forms it can take and the least important of those are physical.”</i><br><br><b>“Who’s Your Daddy?”</b><br><br><a href="http://s1206.photobucket.com/albums/bb447/shawnarazz/?action=view&amp;current=David-Gandy-3-1.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380374277i/728252.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Knight’s Hot in a Suit, Sophisticated Style:<br><br><b>‘Cause every girl crazy ‘bout a Sharp Dressed Man!</b><br><br><a href="http://s1206.photobucket.com/albums/bb447/shawnarazz/?action=view&amp;current=tumblr_lqredpXoPu1qep71v-1.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380374277i/728253.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="http://s1206.photobucket.com/albums/bb447/shawnarazz/?action=view&amp;current=8850lc00xre2880r.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380374277i/728254.jpg" alt="Photobucket" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

<div id="review_642982558" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/642982558" />
    <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts"><img alt="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1378340325p2/17755575.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/642982558?book_show_action=true">Jun 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Wendy&#39;sThoughts" href="/user/show/17755575-wendy-sthoughts">Wendy&#39;sThoughts</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/36146228-knight">review of another edition</a>

          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">KA Fans, Romance, Everyone</span></div>

        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/17755575-wendy-sthoughts?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer642982558" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10089807468631902909"><b>5 Re-Read for the Third Time Stars <br/>* * * * *<i> Spoiler Free </i><br/>There are book men who are so fully formed, they radiate off the pages. They come at you with a power that transcends reading and you feel them before you have read much about them. Yes, there will be a description; details of eyes, hair and build. There will be clothing and ways of moving... whether they are purposeful in their gate or just kind of get to the object of their desire in a rush. All of these details, of course, round out th</b></span>
  <span id="freeText10089807468631902909" style="display:none"><b>5 Re-Read for the Third Time Stars <br>* * * * *<i> Spoiler Free </i><br>There are book men who are so fully formed, they radiate off the pages. They come at you with a power that transcends reading and you feel them before you have read much about them. Yes, there will be a description; details of eyes, hair and build. There will be clothing and ways of moving... whether they are purposeful in their gate or just kind of get to the object of their desire in a rush. All of these details, of course, round out the mental image of the man... but with some, they aren't entirely necessary... and that's because these men come to us... tapping into every physical and mental sense we have...like a subliminal message or call...they are there and we know them. <br><br>Knight is one of those men. Air shifts. He has a force field and those around him sense him coming. This is not superhero bullshit... this is dynamic, controlling, powerful man. If you think this is only in books, ask any female if this type of awareness is possible; every single one of them will tell you, yes....and their eyes will glaze over... they may not have actually interacted with one... but somewhere in their lives... they ran across one and the impact and wishing... still can be recalled. <br><br>This book is a testimony to overcoming horror of all types. He... dealt with situations which marked him to his core... shaped him to protect those he loved and weaker in society. He was smart...old beyond his years... saw too much for a child's vision; so he became a man before his time. It set his path. He appreciated the good that came to him; held on and used what was given him... and made the decision early never to be in a position of others' control again... whether in work or life... He bided his time.... looking for opportunities and then made his moves. <br>Created his world... and those in it learned... You did as Knight instructed. He was loyal, decisive, very smart, and direct.<br><br>The other person in this world is Anya. </b>It would be easy to think she is this woman who was not up to the level of Knight. She had had her own living hell after only being with her parents for seven years... they were killed together in a random carjacking...leaving her to be raised by a cruel and lazy aunt. Yet, Anya had developed an inner strength... recognizing early on... life can be what you make it... you take what is given and figure out a way to make it better somehow. And bless her... she was in the process of doing just that. She was careful with her money; had a business goal and stuck to it no matter what. She had a concrete vision of the goal and worked every day to make it happen. She was extremely smart about her likes/dislikes and worked to create her own ways and style without overthinking it. She understood.... this was her life... there was no safety net or person coming to the rescue... she was it and lived accordingly.<br><br>These two meet through circumstances which could happen in anyone's life... a party, a need to make a call for a taxi. Yet, due to who Knight was and how the situation presented to him... with other surrounding factors... he took it upon himself to intervene and drive her home. Anya becoming an excuse for Knight to collect himself and leave the environment pissing him off is scooped up/ moved along and reasoned with to allow Knight to do this action.<br><br>Was she weak when she didn't stick to her first inclination to say no... or the second time when she explained why it wasn't necessary.... or the third when she tried to insist... no, because as you can see she was trying to reason with him as to why she didn't need him to do it. What developed into a pattern and made this relationship as perfect as it was ... was... she would listen to how he would counter her reasons for something.... and inevitably, Knight would have an answer that made sense... He saw money was tight by her clothes.. not the taste but the quality... he knew the taxi cost would be a hit; he also told her she would be helping him by allowing him to drive off the steam. These were legitimate reasons... also... she sensed the man he was... and at that moment, a decision was made and she went with him.<br><br>It is through this pattern that developed between the two of them we get to follow her thought process... get to hear her mind racing... feeling all of the changes and adjustments. At first... it may feel like she is overwhelmed... and there are moments of that... but as the relationship between them develops... Anya develops more of her understanding of who she is, what she is attracted to... and how Knight is ticking boxes she didn't know she had to tick. Knight also has opened her eyes to how others see her... the reality of her... the beauty of her and how she had no idea about this. <br><br>Knight sees Anya for the miracle she is... unassuming; open, loyal and never expecting anything from anyone. He gives her things and she tries to return them... he makes things easier and she is appreciative... he feeds her.... doesn't make a move on her... and she wishes he did. <br><br>All of this leads up to him laying it out for her... his ways...rules... need for control and punishment with always taking care of her after. He breaks it down, the process by process... makes sense to her internal thoughts and there is also that tingle which keeps curling within her when he talks about all of it. These two finally connect and when they do, we are there... learning and understanding Knight just like Anya... nothing is left to the imagination... and we are either on board... or we should go... yet... the decision was made from the start... we went with him in his car... through his club... and to his home... we went with him because we know he would never hurt us through Anya... because he has shown his sweet... and it is sooooooo good. <br><br>Being with Anya and Knight is a special type of beauty... it is not conventional... it is not something everyone will be comfortable with and that is totally ok... but if you can see your way through to these people and why they are who they are and how perfect they are together... then you will get to experience love on a level few get...whether in books, movies or in your own life... and the thing about this type of love... you do not have to have the money or status that the book has to feel it... you just need to be open to being accepting your partner fully for who they are and love them for it.<br><br>Knight is special... but Anya makes him more so... and it is the coming together of these two which grabs your heart and soul. <br><br>KA took a risk when she went on this journey a few years ago... she has since added to this series with Creed and Raid. She has stated another Unfinished Hero is in the works... hopefully, we will get him soon.<br><br><strong>For more Reviews, Free E-books and Giveaways</strong><br><div>
  <br>
  <a href="http://starangelsreviews.blogspot.com/" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img alt=" photo banner_zpsb3ab83a0.jpg" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1407612151i/10746470._SX540_.jpg" width="400" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
