        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1062589187" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17306101693242565493"><b>5 ohhhhh yeah... daddy STARS</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414450139i/11656279.png' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>I'm sorry it took me a while to write this, but this was my first book by Kristen Ashley (yes, I know I'm late to the party...as usual) and I was struggling to write a review that would do this amazing book justice. So, I hope I accomplished this *cough*minor*cough* task...and for those of you who haven't read <i>Knight</i>...maybe I can give you a little incentive to finally pick it up. I really don't know what you are waiting for. Oh, the review...right. Let's start.<br/><br/>Warnin</span>
  <span id="freeText17306101693242565493" style="display:none"><b>5 ohhhhh yeah... daddy STARS</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414450139i/11656279.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I'm sorry it took me a while to write this, but this was my first book by Kristen Ashley (yes, I know I'm late to the party...as usual) and I was struggling to write a review that would do this amazing book justice. So, I hope I accomplished this *cough*minor*cough* task...and for those of you who haven't read <i>Knight</i>...maybe I can give you a little incentive to finally pick it up. I really don't know what you are waiting for. Oh, the review...right. Let's start.<br><br>Warning: Domineering alpha-male ahead! ;D<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“He might be scary but scary never eradicated hot.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Anya has a problem. No scratch that, Anya has at least three problems. First, the party her friend dragged her to, is way too swank and her dress far too cheap and really the girl just wants to go home. Second problem...her best friend thinks she has found her golden goose and refuses to go home with Anya. Third...she needs to call a taxi, but her phone is dead.<br><br>Now, idem number four on my list can be viewed as a problem or the best coincidence of a lifetime. While searching for a working phone dear Anya stumbles upon Knight, the incredibly angry and scary looking piece of male hotness who, after being pissed that she invaded his bedroom, decides to give her a ride home...mostly against her will, but what's a girl to do? <br><br>Why lucky coincidence? Well, he brings her home safe, saves her the money for a taxi and he drives an Aston Martin. That's just something every girl has to experience in her lifetime and it's quite obvious that he will be the romantic interest, since we are talking about a romance novel...duh! Oh, and did I mention that he wants nothing in return...for now? Right, he is a real gentleman...sort of. So, what does it take? 'Cause Anya is a looker and he would agree. Granted he puts it in his own special way, but I think he likes what he sees.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Babe, your clothes. Shit. But you work ‘em and you do because you’ve got one serious fantastic body, your hair is even better and your face is a face that launches a thousand hard-ons.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Ultimately, Anya has to get into a precarious situation in Knight's night club for him to finally make his move and oh boy....'daddy' has some moves... and the rest is history, as they say. ;D <br><br>Well, it's not that easy and this is only the first few pages of the book, but I'm not willing to share much more. READ THE BOOK!<br><br><br><b>Anya Gage</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414799554i/11694846.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Anya lost both her parents when she was seven years old. Everything after that was a struggle. She lived with her verbally abusive aunt and as soon as Anya was old enough she left and never looked back. Everything she owns, and that is very little, she has earned with hard work and determination. She works full time at an office, goes to beauty school at night and manages to squeeze in a few nail clients in her free time.<br><br>I really liked her as a heroin. She doesn't expect much out of life and everything she accomplishes or later on is gifted to her, she sees a blessing and she never takes anything for granted. <br><br>As one of her best friends Vivica would put it...she was dealt a shitty hand so far, but meeting Knight is the best thing that could happen to her. And Auntie Vivica is someone you need to listen to. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"No matter how bumpy the ride gets, listen to your Auntie Vivica, hold the fuck on."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>She has the best advice and she has no problem to say it like it is. A true friend...seriously, everyone needs a friend like Vivica. But honestly, being with Knight isn't easy...he has secrets and Anya has to make a few concessions in order for this relationship to work. <br><br><br><b>Knight Sebring</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414799554i/11694847.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Knight is a very successful business man, with a highly developed protective instinct. He owns one of the most popular clubs in the city and he drives an Aston Martin. That just tells you all you need to know about his financial status.<br><br>He is also a very secretive man who and I quote 'keeps his shit tight'. Why and how and what will be disclosed later in the book. Quite interesting story and I really think it fit very well with the character.<br><br>Knight is my ultimate book boyfriend. I'm still not sure how it happened, but I'm completely under his spell. He is one scary mother-fucker; he is in control all of the time and talks very little. And when something comes out of his mouth it's usually so wrong and at the same time right that I don't even know where my head is anymore. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“You don't need to like me to let me fuck you but since I like you, I'd prefer it that way.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote> <br>On top of that he is domineering as hell, a dirty talker and he is rough and awesome and I'm in love and all is good in the world...I just totally lost track...<br><br>Knight is also unapologetic about who he is, what he does and he has no need to change. I love that in my book boyfriends. A redemption plotline can be interesting, but usually I want them to be bad and don't play by the rules. This one sure is an anti-hero and I love it.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1414799554i/11694848.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now, Knight and Anya together...holy moley! That's just HAWT! Like seriously scorching. The writing style is very elaborate and with that kind of attention to detail you can lose the reader quite easily in a sex scene, but oh dear...I sure as hell wasn't lost...right there, every second.<br><br>What really surprised me about this book were the sweet moments between Knight and Anya. Yes, he can be sweet...I was shocked too. All in all it is a well rounded, yet slightly unconventional love story and if you like a lot of control in your book boyfriends you really should pick this one up.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>“Honey, the candles are gonna burn out," I prompted on a grin. "Let 'em," he replied. "Got nothin' I want. Everything I want is standing right in front of me.”</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>Since this was my first Kristen Ashley book I have to confess that it took me a while to get into the highly descriptive style and the fact that we have a slow burner here. But in all honesty I didn't care, the story and the characters had me so hooked and I actually read it in one day. Couldn't put it down and it is entirely possible that I didn't listen to my Prof. during that one class. *coughs*<br><br>I've seen many different review and ratings for this book. I guess the biggest issue is the whole 'daddy' thing...oh well...it takes some getting used to. But it's also really hot. For me <i>Knight</i> was a complete success. I don't know why some things just click with me but this one just hit home and I honestly could read twenty more books just like this one. In fact, I already re-read a few scenes and I started with the second book in the <i>Unfinished Hero</i>series. I'm definitely turning into a KA fan...not that I expected anything less. ;D<br><br><br>**I wrote this in a slightly tipsy state...all mistakes are mine! ;D<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1418911509i/12944326.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://coffeeaddictbooks.blogspot.co.at/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1431601625i/14852808.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><a href="https://www.facebook.com/coffeeaddictbooks?ref=tn_tnmn" rel="nofollow noopener">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1297845984" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4467360204205669823"><b>3 STARS! ★★★</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433427249i/15095106.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>“You don’t fuck Knight. No way. Knight fucks you.”</i>
</b><br/><br/>Well this day came sooner than I thought as I've officially popped my KA cherry, woohoo! Y'all can thank my blog wife, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr' rel='nofollow noopener'>Allison</a> who pulled a dirty one on me to get me to pick this one up. Note to self: Do not mess with Allison when it comes to Kristen Ashley, this woman loves her KA fix. Having <u>Knight</u> being one of her all time book husbands, naturally I had to meet him myself to see what's the fuss all about. <br/><br/>All I can say is that </span>
  <span id="freeText4467360204205669823" style="display:none"><b>3 STARS! ★★★</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433427249i/15095106.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>“You don’t fuck Knight. No way. Knight fucks you.”</i>
</b><br><br>Well this day came sooner than I thought as I've officially popped my KA cherry, woohoo! Y'all can thank my blog wife, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/user/show/9080319-allison-will-never-conquer-her-tbr" rel="nofollow noopener">Allison</a> who pulled a dirty one on me to get me to pick this one up. Note to self: Do not mess with Allison when it comes to Kristen Ashley, this woman loves her KA fix. Having <u>Knight</u> being one of her all time book husbands, naturally I had to meet him myself to see what's the fuss all about. <br><br>All I can say is that Knight is the definition of ultimate Alpha-male with a capital A. I'm super positive that in all of my reading experience, no one can probably top him in this department. Grade A possessive, dominant alpha male who is an absolute control-freak that will go all full-on protective mode on the woman he loves. <br><br>I'm not gonna lie, that's pretty damn hot to read about. Also I found Knight to be a rather amusing character because he came off like an oxymoron; caveman-like but yet such a gentleman. He can be an arse but still be a sweetheart. In a way, that makes him rather swoon-worthy because who doesn't want a man packed with helluva testosterones to utter goddamn sweet words to the woman he cares about deeply? Yup I get it now Allison, he's a keeper for sure ;)<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427478435i/14274945.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>So the thing about this book...well I didn't hate it but I didn't love it either. There were just so many little things that bugged me throughout. I thought the first half of the book piqued my interest with this thing going on between Anya and Knight but having read more on later, all I got was a pretty routined life of them going at each other. I'm not even gonna talk about how this was almost instalove at its best with Knight being fixated with Anya within minutes of finding her in his room. Or how Anya somehow willingly does every single thing he says when she barely knows him. There were some minor drama scenes that got thrown into the mix but it just left me feeling all meh about it. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1433430752ra/15095700.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>My major struggle would definitely be the dialogue between both Anya and Knight, especially Knight. His slang(?) or clipped sentences drove me completely nuts till at some point, I kinda gave up trying to decipher his sentences. It was a whole lot of weirdly structured sentences with multiple commas and throw in several f-bombs in between. <br><br>Apparently I've been told that this is a common thing in KA's alpha males, so maybe it needs to take quite some time getting used to. Also there were just a whole lot of 'babe' and 'honey' being thrown back and forth, can't exactly say those are my cuppas in the endearment department. <br><br>And now to address the big elephant in the room, those who may or may not know about this particular book or dare I say, a usage of a peculiar term. Yup it's that baby/Daddy thing. Personally I didn't find it to be a complete turn-off but I wasn't a fan of it either because I just found it to be so...out of place? It's like one of those moments where I read a scene and all of a sudden this comes up -&gt; <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[
  <i>
    <b>"My baby wants her Daddy."</b>
  </i>
 <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> that had me going "Did that just REALLY happened?" and I'd be having this incredulous look trying to take it all in. It was just all kinds of weird for me but I can see how it'll work for some people.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1381353248ra/4749761.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But the steam though, WOWZA. KA sure as hell can write some might fine sex scenes that would be hazardous to all Kindles alike. Added on with an ultimate alpha male and dirty talker like Knight, a precaution would surely be required. <br><br>The revelation at the end, well I can't say that I'm shocked by it. It does leave me a little iffy with how Anya seemed to be rather complacent about finding out the truth and just let the matter pass without much ado. I probably got it that the reveal of Knight's true nature is what makes up the anti-hero part of him but perhaps it would have left a bigger impact had it been uncovered much earlier in the read. <br><br>But I still want to applaud the author for making Knight an anti-hero through and through. He was unapologetic of the way he is and just laid it all out for Anya to accept and love him for who he truly is. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“You gotta know that every second I spend with you it becomes more and more clear you were made for me. A gift I don’t deserve, didn’t earn but I’m not giving back.”</i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427478435i/14274945.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Overall I'm rather indifferent about this one. Sorry Allison and to all my KA ladies who loved this!! :( I tried and while I did enjoy it at some parts, perhaps this just wasn't really for me. However I do have a knack for her badass alpha males, so I'll definitely be checking out her other series still :) Keep the KA recs coming! ♥<br><br><i><u>Knight</u> is the first book in the Unfinished Hero series and can be read as a standalone.</i><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427351718i/14265304.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><a href="http://readescapadereviews.blogspot.com/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427480966i/14275361.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.facebook.com/readingescapadeblog" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427480966i/14275362.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://twitter.com/readingescapade" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1427480966i/14275363.png" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> </["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Vika aka ♔ of GIF &amp; Grumpy Smut-ateer *P/T Freebie Fairy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Vika aka ♔ of GIF &amp; Grumpy Smut-ateer *P/T Freebie Fairy" href="/user/show/7690153-vika-aka-of-gif-grumpy-smut-ateer-p-t-freebie-fairy">Vika aka ♔ of GIF &amp; Grumpy Smut-ateer *P/T Freebie Fairy</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1719947801" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer563593043111626757">Find all of my reviews at: <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/'>http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/</a><br/><br/><a href='http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1470932507ra/19982798.gif' alt='commercial photography locations' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/><i>Knight</i> popped up on my radar due to <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1715233216?book_show_action=false&from_review_page=1' rel='nofollow noopener'>Camilla’s</a> updates. By the time I realized this might not be my perfect porny match it was too late and the library copy had been uploaded to the ol’ Kindle. Here’s the crazy part: This book had me freaking <b>hooked</b>. It was full of OTT alpha speak and instalove and bossypants and dialogue like this . . . <br/><br/><b>
  <i>“That teeters over the edge of macho crazy, Knight,” I informed him.<br/><br/>“Yeah,” he was completely</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText563593043111626757" style="display:none">Find all of my reviews at: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/">http://52bookminimum.blogspot.com/</a><br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1470932507ra/19982798.gif" alt="commercial photography locations" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><i>Knight</i> popped up on my radar due to <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1715233216?book_show_action=false&amp;from_review_page=1" rel="nofollow noopener">Camilla’s</a> updates. By the time I realized this might not be my perfect porny match it was too late and the library copy had been uploaded to the ol’ Kindle. Here’s the crazy part: This book had me freaking <b>hooked</b>. It was full of OTT alpha speak and instalove and bossypants and dialogue like this . . . <br><br><b>
  <i>“That teeters over the edge of macho crazy, Knight,” I informed him.<br><br>“Yeah,” he was completely not offended. “Heads up, babe, get used to that.”</i>
</b><br><br>And I was all . . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1470932507ra/19982799.gif" alt="commercial photography locations" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>#nomnomnomnom<br><br>Now here’s a super random confession for you – even though Knight is <i>clearly</i> described as a reincarnated god of some sort, in my head I pictured Nathan Fillion the entire time . . . <br><br><a href="http://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1470932890ra/19982833.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>I know, right? Whatever. Apparently my pervy brain thinks he would be a boss in the bedroom *shrug*.<br><br>Alright, so the story is about Anya – a woman who had a shitty childhood (due to her parents dying and not some tropey bad sexual experience bullcrap like usual) and is now going to school in the evenings and working by day in order to one day hopefully own her own spa. Anya gets roped in to attending a party with her wretched whore of a friend (read the book and then tell me you don’t feel the same) who promptly chooses a bro before her ho, forcing Anya to cab it home. While attempting to call a cab, Anya accidentally chooses an occupied room. Said occupant? Our leading male. He tells Anya he’ll take her home and then basically won't get the hell out of her life. (Yes, totally like a creepy stalker but since he was super bangable it made it A-okay.)<br><br>Knight makes it crystal clear he’s not your Average Joe . . . <br><br><b>
  <i>“You, Anya, are a woman who needs a dog, a house with a white picket fence, one boy, one girl, and a man who worships the ground you walk on, thanks God every night he was fuckin’ lucky enough to con you into lyin’ your head on the pillow beside his, but still watches football on Sundays. You and me stay the course, you are never gonna get that from me.”</i>
</b><br><br>And then someone must have spilled a glass of water in my underwears or something.<br><br>Now, of course since this was a Kristen Ashley story things couldn’t just stay splooshtastic. First we had to learn about Anya’s body image issue – built like Jessica Rabbit, but with a tummy pooch . . . <br><br><a href="http://lunapic.com" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1470932507ra/19982801.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>First world problems.<br><br>I was okay with it, though, because nearly <b>everyone</b> has body issues even if they are pert near perfect.<br><br>I was even on board with the Bossy Betty stuff and thought KA did a good job making even a vanilla gal like me good with the control dealio.<br><br>But then?????<br><br><b>
  <i>“Baby wants her Daddy.”</i>
</b><br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1470932507ra/19982802.gif" alt="commercial photography locations" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>NOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOOPE.</b> <br><br>This could’ve been 4, but helltothenah on the daddy talk. That dried up the lady garden post haste!<br><br><br><b>ORIGINAL "REVIEW":</b><br><br>So apparently this features "Daddy" talk . . . . <br><br><a href="http://www.freeimagehosting.net/commercial-photography/" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1470427389ra/19928254.gif" alt="commercial photography locations" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Send prayers. Or tequila. Actually, just tequila.</span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">fans of Fifty Shades</span></div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer439333947" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9017733832380473271"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395113i/760856._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395113i/760857._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Holy freakin' hotness.<br/><br/>So, I'm thinking I might need therapy some time soon. I'm beginning to get slightly depressed that men are just <i>sooo</i> much better in books than they are in real life! Especially in KA books!<br/><br/>Knight. Oh. My. Actual. God! Where does she come up with this stuff?! Knight is the <i>ultimate</i> alpha! And he's called <i>Knight</i>!!!<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Um, I don't know your name but -"<br/>"Knight,"<br/>"Right, Mr. Knight-"<br/>"No, Knight."<br/>"That's what I said, Knight. Now, Mr. Knight-"<br/>"No, not Mr. Knight. Knight. My na</i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText9017733832380473271" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395113i/760856._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395113i/760857._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Holy freakin' hotness.<br><br>So, I'm thinking I might need therapy some time soon. I'm beginning to get slightly depressed that men are just <i>sooo</i> much better in books than they are in real life! Especially in KA books!<br><br>Knight. Oh. My. Actual. God! Where does she come up with this stuff?! Knight is the <i>ultimate</i> alpha! And he's called <i>Knight</i>!!!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Um, I don't know your name but -"<br>"Knight,"<br>"Right, Mr. Knight-"<br>"No, Knight."<br>"That's what I said, Knight. Now, Mr. Knight-"<br>"No, not Mr. Knight. Knight. My name is Knight."<br>"Your Christian name is Knight?"<br>"If that means first name, yeah."<br>"With a 'K'?"<br>"Yeah, babe, with a 'K'."<br>"That's an unusual name."<br>"Yeah."<br>"I kind of like it."<br>"I can die happy."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>And why, oh why, do I want to bow down and lick the flesh of a man who is, by his own admission, violent, controlling and runs in a world of corruption and badness?!!! It's wrong. I know that my moral compass is askew and I'm feeling that I should feel bad about that. But I totally don't.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395113i/760858._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Ok, let's lay it out... if my actual-real-life boyfriend went out and had someone beaten-the-shit-out-of for me, yeh, I would flip my shit. If he told me I wasn't allowed to dance on a dance floor in a club, again, serious diva stropping would ensue! But this isn't real life, right?<br>This is a hot, alpha male, dominant man, fantasy book boyfriend and that makes it okay for me to love Knight.<br><br>And I do. I really really do. I love Knight Sebring. He is possibly one of my favourite alpha males. Ev-er!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I find all of this very confusing."<br>"You get in my bed, I'll sort you out."<br>"You're that good?"<br>"Yeah, I am, baby. I will take care of you there in all the ways you need me to do it. That I can guarantee."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>So, let's talk about <i>Knight</i>. The book, not the character. Anya is skint. She works hard for the little money she earns, lives in a sub-standard apartment, has a day job, an evening job and goes to school. Her world is turned upside down when she accidentally wanders into Knight's room and pisses him off! Still, even pissed he can't ignore how attracted he is to her. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Babe, your clothes. Shit. But you work 'em and you do because you've got one serious fantastic body, your hair is even better and your face is a face that launches a thousand hard-ons."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>After trying to stay away, cut a long story short, he can't and eventually Anya finds herself in a relationship she never saw coming and isn't sure she even agreed to. But, again, she can't deny that she is attracted to and intrigued by the mean and moody Knight. And so it begins...<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I get this this is intense because I'm intense, that's the whole fuckin' deal. I get it'll take you a while to get used to it. But you want it. Fuck, you even like it. You just don't understand it yet. But you will."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>This book really seems to have split opinions right down the middle, so, naturally, I was curious. I know a lot of people really didn't like the way Knight speaks, the way he is with Anya, etc. Also, he calls Anya his baby and has her call him 'Daddy'... now, I will admit, this is something I am not entirely comfortable with. The whole Daddy thing does <i>not</i> do it for me. In the slightest. However, I kind of just looked past it... it's part of Anya and Knight and it works for them. Just because it doesn't tickle <i>my</i> pickle, doesn't mean I can't enjoy their story.<br><br>I also get why people might have problems with Knight. He is controlling to the point of it being totally wrong! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395113i/760859._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And Anya just kind of gets on with it. Again, I have to stress, just because I enjoyed this book, it doesn't mean I condone this type of behaviour in real life. But there is no getting away from the fact that I found Knight hot as all get out! He can also be soooo incredibly sweet.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"Toasted almond pancakes. Sweet soft 'okays'. Makin' me laugh more in a few weeks than I have in decades. 'Yes, Daddys' I feel in my dick. The first voicemail you left me, babe, I saved it and I listen to it once a day. If I lose focus, I see you on your back, knees high, legs wide, offering your sweet, wet pussy to me. You smile at me in bed every time you wander outta my bedroom in my shirts, my tees or your work clothes and honest to Christ, it sets me up for the day. And no matter what shit goes down, I get through it knowin' whichever bed I climb into at night, you're in it ready to snuggle into me or give me what I wanna take. Your girl, a headache. You, never. And in a life that's been full of headaches, babe, having that, there is no price tag. You gotta get it and do it right fuckin' now that there's a lotta different kinds of give and take. And you give as good as you get, baby, trust me."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>And I almost melted when he said...<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"She's beautiful, Dad. You see her, you won't believe your eyes. You'll think you're dreamin'."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>This book was kinda like Kristen Ashley's very own <i>Fifty Shades</i>. Knight is Christian Grey, badass KA style! And if that doesn't send you into a spin... I don't know what will?! <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You please me, I'll please you. You do what I tell you to do, I'll take care of you. You disobey me or act out, I'll punish you then I'll take care of you."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Filthy rich, night-club and real estate owning, impeccably dressed, demanding, moody, likes-to-tie-you-up-and-spank-you, not-very-likeable-atall, but totally, undeniably hotter than hades... ringing any bells? That's Knight. Well, and Christian Grey... but, right now, this is Knight.<br><br><span>[image error]</span><br><br>For Kristen Ashley virgins... you neeeeed to read these books! KA is the Goddess of writing shit hot alpha badboys. Her writing is so identifiable and it can take a little bit of getting used to. KA character's dialogue is instantly recognisable and a little confusing at times. But so soooo good. Seriously. Get some KA in your life.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You don't fuck Knight. No way. Knight fucks you."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>And out of all her books, I think this might just be my favourite!! I can't wait to read <i>Creed</i> and <i>Raid</i>!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380395113i/760861._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b><i>Knight</i> Statistics</b><br><b>Steam Rating (out of 5):</b> ♥♥♥♥♥<br><b>Ending:</b> HEA<br><b>Series:</b> ✓ <br><b>Reading Order: </b><br>Book #1 - Knight<br>Book #2 - Creed<br>Book #3 - Raid<br><b>Can this be read as a standalone?</b> Yes<br><b>Themes:</b><br>Rich hero<br>BDSM<br>Controlling alpha male<br><b>Warning. This book includes...</b> <br>Graphic sexual content<br>BDSM<br>A hero like marmite!<br><b>Writing:</b> Fantastic<br><br>UK AMAZON: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.amazon.co.uk/Knight-Unfinished-Hero-Series-ebook/dp/B007SFBPFY/ref=sr_1_1?ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1371903719&amp;sr=8-1&amp;keywords=knight+kristen+ashley">http://www.amazon.co.uk/Knight-Unfini...</a><br>US AMAZON: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.amazon.com/Knight-Unfinished-Hero-Series-ebook/dp/B007SFBPFY/ref=sr_1_1?ie=UTF8&amp;qid=1371903719&amp;sr=8-1&amp;keywords=knight+kristen+ashley">http://www.amazon.com/Knight-Unfinish...</a><br><br><b>

    <a title="~Stéphanie&#39;s Journal~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/24323583-st-phanie-s-journal"><img alt="~Stéphanie&#39;s Journal~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1567153083p2/24323583.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1090400080?book_show_action=true">Oct 27, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~Stéphanie&#39;s Journal~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~Stéphanie&#39;s Journal~" href="/user/show/24323583-st-phanie-s-journal">~Stéphanie&#39;s Journal~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1090400080" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6602590387433893323"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433240653i/15069972.jpg' width='400' height='310' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>It's been a long time since I wanted to read one of Kristen Ashley book. This week end was finally the time to meet one of her hot alpha male and I decided to go for Knight.<br/><br/>I love a hot alpha dominant male and with him I got my catch! What attracted me to him was his anti-hero side. <br/><br/>I know a lot of you have already read this book so I won't probably go into the details but for someone who has never read a KA book or if you are undecided about <b>Knight</b>, you have to know that the guy is certainly th</span>
  <span id="freeText6602590387433893323" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433240653i/15069972.jpg" width="400" height="310" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It's been a long time since I wanted to read one of Kristen Ashley book. This week end was finally the time to meet one of her hot alpha male and I decided to go for Knight.<br><br>I love a hot alpha dominant male and with him I got my catch! What attracted me to him was his anti-hero side. <br><br>I know a lot of you have already read this book so I won't probably go into the details but for someone who has never read a KA book or if you are undecided about <b>Knight</b>, you have to know that the guy is certainly the most alpha male I've EVER read about!<br><br>I will summarize this with one quote:<br><br><b>
  <i>« It’s time you learn something about me, Anya. I don’t live in your world. I live in another world. It’s my world. I took it over. I rebuilt it. I own it. I control it. I have a code. Anyone in my world lives by my code....You do not fuck with what’s mine. »</i>
</b><br><br>If you are not ready to accept that you won't probably like him.<br><br>At first Knight made me laugh so much. His caveman and macho ways were so funny for me. When he says something, you have to listen but I'm such a bad girl I would have been more a pain in his ass.<br><br>When he <u> decides </u> to have Anya, it's not to let her walk away easily.<br><br><b>« Babe, come here.”<br>Was he high?<br>“No, I’m leaving,” I fired back.<br>“You don’t wanna walk away from me.”<br>My brows shot up. “I don’t?”<br>“No.”<br>“Wrong,” I retorted. “I do. Sorry,” I went on then finished, “Good-bye Knight.”<br>Then, as I heard movers coming back, I turned to round the wall of the kitchen.<br>I got one step in. Then I was not only in the kitchen but across it, my back pressed to the counter and Knight pressed into me. »</b><br><br>But there's so much more to him being all dominant. Knight is also sweet and very caring. This side of him made me swoon. Knight gives the world to his woman and you only want to give him the world.<br><br>I had more problems with<b> Anya</b>. She is twenty seven but I would have given her barely twenty. She was kind of silly sometimes. I get she had a difficult life but her reactions were a little too immature for her age.<br><br>Them <b>as a couple was a perfect match</b>! They connect the moment their met. Knight tries to stay away but it's impossible to resist when Anya put herself in a difficult position.<br><br>Their strength together is probably trust. Knight is very open to explain everything to her. All she has to do is ask a question and he will answer honestly. For me in this kind of relationship, where you have a guy who is so much into control, it's important to have honesty and trust. As both are a big part of this book, I could only be happy to see their feelings grow and become love.<br><br><b>
  <i>« You stick by me, you, and only you, will learn why I am how I am. No one knows. No one. But you, Anya, you stick with me, I’ll share. And right now, bonus. I’ll tell you what you already know but you don’t understand. I like control and I have a temper. I see the world a certain way. I want my world a certain way. And I set about getting it. If I don’t, if I can’t control that, harness it, things can get ugly. So I do. When I do, say when I’m punishing you, I never lose control because what I’m doing is a release. And the only time I’ll lose control is when I’m finally inside you and you’ll like that, I promise you. »</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433240653i/15069973._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="559" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Now Kristen Ashley's writing was absolutely delicious! What I liked the most was how she gives every detail, every word an importance. Sometimes books lack words to describe the way you feel when you enter a room, when you are in a particular situation. But with KA, it's certainly not the case! It's like you are in the book and in the hero or heroine's head, you see with their eyes.<br>In the same aspect, the sex scenes smoking hot! Once again, as a couple Knight and Anya are perfect! They respond to each other in an incredible way. The attraction, the combination of want and need is so powerful; you will only want to devour this book!<br><br>When I closed the book, I only wanted to jump in another marvellous book from KA. I know I said in my updates than the next one would probably be The Mystery Man or The Gamble but after I read Creed's blurb, I think I'm going to change my mind a continue with the Unfinished Heroes series ♥<br><br><b>Knight: 4.5 stars<br>Anya: 3 stars<br>Writing: 4 stars<br>Hotness: 5 stars</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1433240653i/15069974._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="533" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><a href="http://belgiannaughtyreader.blogspot.be/" rel="nofollow noopener"> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423395446i/13619201.jpg" width="400" height="85" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><a href="https://twitter.com/StephanieonGR" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423556409i/13643591.png" width="53" height="57" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <a href="https://www.facebook.com/belgiannaugthyreader69" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1423556409i/13643592.png" width="53" height="57" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer921803337" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11952707138776984943"><b>Sale Alert: 12Sept17 Kindle Daily Deal <a href='https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B007SFBPFY/ref=s9_acsd_hps_bw_c_x_3_w?pf_rd_m=ATVPDKIKX0DER&pf_rd_s=merchandised-search-2&pf_rd_r=GBV6F3PRSZT4RZ2RFP0R&pf_rd_r=GBV6F3PRSZT4RZ2RFP0R&pf_rd_t=101&pf_rd_p=01360c89-e464-4040-8e10-4907b952e154&pf_rd_p=01360c89-e464-4040-8e10-4907b952e154&pf_rd_i=11552285011' rel='nofollow noopener'>$1.59</a></b> This was my very first ever KA book that sent the ball rolling in the 50ish or so books I've read by her. She is totally my book crack.<br/><br/><b>3.5 Yeah Daddy Stars </b><br/><br/>Reread with my girls at <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148164-buddies-books-and-baubles' rel='nofollow noopener'>Buddies Books and Baubles.</a><br/><br/>I might have liked this a smidge more on read #2<br/><br/>Mature content 18+<br/><br/><b>Knight</b> is not your everyday hero. He is all man and knows exactly who he is, what he wants and what he expects from those around him. Things go his way and when they don’t he remedies</span>
  <span id="freeText11952707138776984943" style="display:none"><b>Sale Alert: 12Sept17 Kindle Daily Deal <a href="https://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B007SFBPFY/ref=s9_acsd_hps_bw_c_x_3_w?pf_rd_m=ATVPDKIKX0DER&amp;pf_rd_s=merchandised-search-2&amp;pf_rd_r=GBV6F3PRSZT4RZ2RFP0R&amp;pf_rd_r=GBV6F3PRSZT4RZ2RFP0R&amp;pf_rd_t=101&amp;pf_rd_p=01360c89-e464-4040-8e10-4907b952e154&amp;pf_rd_p=01360c89-e464-4040-8e10-4907b952e154&amp;pf_rd_i=11552285011" rel="nofollow noopener">$1.59</a></b> This was my very first ever KA book that sent the ball rolling in the 50ish or so books I've read by her. She is totally my book crack.<br /><br /><b>3.5 Yeah Daddy Stars </b><br /><br />Reread with my girls at <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/group/show/148164-buddies-books-and-baubles" rel="nofollow noopener">Buddies Books and Baubles.</a><br /><br />I might have liked this a smidge more on read #2<br /><br />Mature content 18+<br /><br /><b>Knight</b> is not your everyday hero. He is all man and knows exactly who he is, what he wants and what he expects from those around him. Things go his way and when they don’t he remedies that situation no matter who he has to hurt. <b>Anya</b> has been beaten down by others most her life. She lost her parents young and has never had anyone really care about or take care of her. She is self sufficient has her goals for her life and is working toward them. But when Knight starts doing things to take care of her without asking for anything in return she is drawn into him and his control.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>“Wars fought over a face like this.” He murmured like he was talking to himself. My heart stopped beating and his thumbs moved lightly across my cheeks. “A man would work himself into the ground for it, go down to his knees to beg to keep it, endure torture to protect it, take a bullet for it,” his eyes came to mine, “poison his brother to possess a face like this.”</i>
</b><br /><br />There are quite a few moments when Knight is endearing like this. But there are plenty of other moments when he is laying down the law. He is one of Kristen Ashley’s uber alpha males and as such he is sometimes a little over the top. He is in everyway a Dom and even though Anya has never had an experience in the role of submissive she finds that her introduction into his world to be exciting and maybe what she has always wanted.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>”I have a new boyfriend. He’s awesome. Protective. And scary. And he regularly freaks me out by being all of those at once.”</i>
</b><br /><br />Kristin Ashley(KA) is an author I have to be in the mood for. The OTT alphaness of the heroes of her series is something I crave at times, but <b>I need to be in the mood for it or my feminism overtakes the enjoyment of the story</b>. KA also has a tendency to use dialogue words that I think somewhat uncharacteristic of a romance. Okay, Yeah daddy, Good baby and Fuck me being the ones used the most in this novel. Also the lingo from Knight in this reminded me of maybe a New Jersey clipped dialect, or what I imagine that to me since I live in Utah and have no real idea how people from Jersey talk.<br /><br />That said it really worked for Knight and the antihero he is. I don’t think I’ve ever read anything with a ‘Who’s your daddy’ type theme but remarkably it worked for this and I didn’t mind it at all, enjoyed many parts of it *feminist side hangs head in shame*. I liked the way that Knight treated Anya, she is precious to him and he would protect her from everything in the world if he could, including himself and her past demons.<br /><br /><b>
  <i>No, Anya, no fucked up shit outta that sweet mouth. I’m not gonna listen to it and I’ll work my balls off, I don’t care if it takes decades, to make you stop even thinkin’ it. Instead, you gotta know that every second I spend with you it becomes more and more clear you were made for me. A gift I don’t deserve, didn’t earn, but I’m not giving it back.”</i>
</b><br /><br />Knight is one of my new favorite antiheros (nobody beats Barrons from the fever Series) and this was an interesting look into a Dom/Sub relationship. I especially liked that all of the characters were late twenties early thirties and not tweens. When you are in the mood for a sexy antihero with OTT alphaness to him give Knight a try.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11952707138776984943" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1460712900" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1460712900" />
    <a title="Ophelia&#39;s Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/47653844-ophelia-s-book-blog"><img alt="Ophelia&#39;s Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1448312511p2/47653844.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1460712900?book_show_action=true">Dec 05, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ophelia&#39;s Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ophelia&#39;s Book Blog" href="/user/show/47653844-ophelia-s-book-blog">Ophelia&#39;s Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/47653844-ophelia-s-book-blog?shelf=review">review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/47653844-ophelia-s-book-blog?shelf=want-in-paperback">want-in-paperback</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1460712900" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15051748263548853466"><p>
  
    <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451084067i/17504967.jpg' alt='41S8guclCUL._SX329_BO1,204,203,200_' width='104' height='157' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
  
</p><br/><p>
  <strong><a href='http://amzn.to/1U8QRzq' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>Knight</a> by Kristen Ashley</strong>
</p><br/><p>
  <strong>Erotic, Captivating and Emotional</strong>, <strong>Kristen Ashley</strong> wrote a <strong>hot</strong>, possessive, controlling <strong>Alpha antihero</strong> that you’ll adore and a fierce, strong yet submissive woman that brings him to his knees.
</p><br/><p>
  I’m a huge Kristen Ashley fan, I read and LOVED many of her books, they’re my go to during reading slumps and bookish hangovers. Mystery Man sits comfortably on my list of TOP Book Boyfriends and Husbands, so naturally I expected a lot out of Knight but at the s</p></span>
  <span id="freeText15051748263548853466" style="display:none"><p>
  
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1451084067i/17504967.jpg" alt="41S8guclCUL._SX329_BO1,204,203,200_" width="104" height="157" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  
</p><br><p>
  <strong><a href="http://amzn.to/1U8QRzq" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">Knight</a> by Kristen Ashley</strong>
</p><br><p>
  <strong>Erotic, Captivating and Emotional</strong>, <strong>Kristen Ashley</strong> wrote a <strong>hot</strong>, possessive, controlling <strong>Alpha antihero</strong> that you’ll adore and a fierce, strong yet submissive woman that brings him to his knees.
</p><br><p>
  I’m a huge Kristen Ashley fan, I read and LOVED many of her books, they’re my go to during reading slumps and bookish hangovers. Mystery Man sits comfortably on my list of TOP Book Boyfriends and Husbands, so naturally I expected a lot out of Knight but at the same time I was nervous because she said that this series is different than her other books, as in darker and more erotic.
</p><br><p>
  Well, let me tell you Knight did not disappoint! I had butterflies in my stomach and my heart was pounding while reading this book, I LOVED it!
</p><br><br><blockquote>
  <br>
  <p>
    
      <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1449499166i/17293176.png" alt="766520" width="68" height="56" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
      
        <strong>“Wars fought over a face like this,” he murmured like he was talking to himself, my heart stopped beating and his thumbs moved lightly across my cheeks. “A man would work himself into the ground for it, go down to his knees to beg to keep it, endure torture to protect it, take a bullet for it,” his eyes came to mine, “Poison his brother to possess a face like this.”</strong>
      
      <br>
    
  </p>
  <br>
</blockquote><br><p>
  Swooooon ♥♥<br>
</p><br><p>
  Knight was not a bad boy. He was a<strong> bad man</strong> he knew who he was, what he wanted and what he liked. And he got it. Period. Law and society be damned. He made his own rules and morals.
</p><br><p>
  I loved him to pieces, I disliked some of his choices in life namely his profession BUT that’s what makes the ANTI in antihero. By no means was he a good normal citizen but he loved Anya and his past justified his actions.
</p><br><p>
  Tortured with a dark past that he keeps secret, he tries to stay away from Anya so she can get the normal life she deserves with the white picket fence and 2 point O kids. But he ends up getting drawn to her and eventually he caves in and decides to be her man.
</p><br><p>
  Knight was very controlling to the point where he dictated what she should wear where she can go and who she associates with. Their relationship has a touch of BDSM. When she disobeyed he punished her (Spanking and such) so if you’re not comfortable with that fair warning.
</p><br><p>
  Anya a <strong>strong independent woman</strong>, was abandoned many times during her short life so she had insecurities and she learned that the only person she can count on is herself, she had her little dream and worked day and night to achieve it. She didn’t expect handouts and refused them when Knight offered. When they got together she became very submissive, she didn’t let go of her dream but she allowed Knight to help her.
</p><br><p>
  Their relationship was <strong>very endearing</strong>, he treated her as his <strong>queen</strong> and she as her <strong>king,</strong> they loved each other deeply and it showed through their words, actions and thoughts. There were no stupid misunderstandings, they communicated very openly with each other which I loved.
</p><br><p>
  The secondary characters were very well developed I loved Vivicia, Anya’s best friend, she was so badass and fierce! I would have loved for her to get a book but she already got her happy ending in this one. The trademark Kristen Ashley Language was there as was the great banter!
</p><br><br><blockquote>
  <br>
  <p>
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1449499166i/17293176.png" alt="766520" width="69" height="57" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
    
      <strong>“Men understand direct communication. It's bitches who speak in code.”</strong>
    
  </p>
  <br>
</blockquote><br><p>
  There was ONE thing that bothered me very much but I eventually got used to it or just pretended it wasn’t there lol I know very mature of me. I’ll put it in the spoiler section because I’m very anti-spoiler even the little things count. It’s about what they call each other during sex.
</p><br><p>
  Minor spoiler:
</p><br><p>
  
    <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[OMFG I hated the fact that she called him Daddy and he called her my Baby EWW!! So not my thing. Shudder.<a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span> <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>
  
</p><br><p>
  Major spoiler: 
</p><br><p>
  
    <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[I HATED HATED HATED the fact that he was a pimp L but I understood given his mother was one and he felt like the girls were going to do it anyway so he may as well provide a safe environment for it. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>
  
</p><br><br><div>
  <br>
  <div>
    <br>
    <div>
      <br>
      <div>
        <br>
        <blockquote>
          <br>
          <div>
            <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1449499166i/17293176.png" alt="766520" width="70" height="58" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
            
              <strong>“You’re perfect, baby.”</strong>
            
            <br>
            
              <strong> I blinked. Then I whispered, “Knight – “</strong>
            
            <br>
            
              <strong> “No, Anya, no fucked up shit outta that sweet mouth. I’m not gonna listen to it and I’ll work my balls off, I don’t care if it takes decades, to make you stop even thinkin’ it. Instead, you gotta know that every second I spend with you it becomes more and more clear that you were made for me. A gift I don’t deserve, didn’t earn but I’m not giving it back.”</strong>
            
          </div>
        </blockquote>
        <br>
      </div>
      <br>
    </div>
    <br>
  </div>
  <br>
</div><br><p>
  <strong>
    Overall it was 4++ Stars read for me. Definitely recommend it!  You’ll keep turning the pages no doubt!
  </strong>
</p><br><p>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer930709808" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10573576329873288357"><i>Reread-5/10/15 Still amazing!<br/>Reread-12/20/15 man will I ever love this book less? No.</i><br/><br/><br/><b>5 'My <i>Knight</i> In Shinning Armer' Stars</b><br/><br/><a href='http://s40.photobucket.com/user/rag/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zps2jymrvvt.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428210035i/14388395._SY540_.jpg' alt=' photo image_zps2jymrvvt.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>First things first, I wanna thank Sofia for recommending this book to me. It's been in my TBR shelf for god knows how long. If it wasn't for you I would've never gotten to it until who knows when. And also welcome to Rag's family baby. <b>Welcome!</b><br/><a href='http://reactiongifs.com/?p=20973' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1402224794ra/9909436.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Anya learned from a very young age that things are not handed to you. You have to bust your ass to earn what you want. She has</span>
  <span id="freeText10573576329873288357" style="display:none"><i>Reread-5/10/15 Still amazing!<br>Reread-12/20/15 man will I ever love this book less? No.</i><br><br><br><b>5 'My <i>Knight</i> In Shinning Armer' Stars</b><br><br><a href="http://s40.photobucket.com/user/rag/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zps2jymrvvt.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>First things first, I wanna thank Sofia for recommending this book to me. It's been in my TBR shelf for god knows how long. If it wasn't for you I would've never gotten to it until who knows when. And also welcome to Rag's family baby. <b>Welcome!</b><br><a href="http://reactiongifs.com/?p=20973" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1402224794ra/9909436.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Anya learned from a very young age that things are not handed to you. You have to bust your ass to earn what you want. She has no exceptions or dreams in life.<br><br><a href="http://s40.photobucket.com/user/rag/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zpsmjkc8sif.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1428210035i/14388396._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo image_zpsmjkc8sif.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>She's at a party that she got dragged to by her best friend because she's chasing after her flavor of the week. So when she couldn't take it anymore she decided that it was time to go home. Funny shit happens and she meets Knight. <br><br><b>“My name is Knight.”<br><br> “Your Christian name is Knight?”<br><br>“If that means first name, yeah,”</b><br><br>Knight is a rich club owner. He is very mysterious. Very intimidating but hot. <i>Daddy Hot.</i> He drops her off and gets more angry over god knows what and leaves. Anya can't stop thinking about him, so when fate bring them together again they seize the opportunity by grabbing on tightly and not letting go.<br><br><b>“I have a new boyfriend. He’s awesome. Protective. And scary. And he regularly freaks me out by being all of those at once.”</b><br><br>When stuff starts to reveal itself, are they gripping tightly?<br><br><b>“I find all of this very confusing,” I admitted cautiously.<br>“You get in my bed, I’ll sort”</b><br><br>Knight. My knight in shinning armer. My savor. My love.my heart. My <i>daddy</i>.<br><br> <a href="http://s40.photobucket.com/user/rag/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zpsr1vtkvkb.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>This book was <i>HOT!</i>. Some people might be disturbed by the whole 'Daddy' concept but nah ah, not this thing over her. I find it hot.<br><br><a href="http://s40.photobucket.com/user/rag/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zpsl8j48qdg.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br><a href="http://reactiongifs.com/?p=17038" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1402279838ra/9915962.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Btw, I don't know what happened to me in this book. Every time someone said the word 'Daddy' Usher pops in my mind with his song "Hey Daddy" if you don't know that song go listen to it. Love it. <br>Anyways over all AMAZING!<br><br><a href="http://s40.photobucket.com/user/rag/media/Mobile%20Uploads/image_zpsvwuwl43d.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_308508832" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/308508832" />
    <a title="Auntee" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/886675-auntee"><img alt="Auntee" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1281897695p2/886675.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/308508832?book_show_action=true">Apr 07, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Auntee" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Auntee" href="/user/show/886675-auntee">Auntee</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">Fans of Kristen Ashley; fans of emotionally tortured heroes</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Auntee by: </span>
      Viv
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=keepers">keepers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=e-books">e-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=2013_reads">2013_reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/886675-auntee?shelf=erotic-romance">erotic-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer308508832" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15413658050358696025"><i>I have to get my thoughts about this book down right now before time dilutes my feelings</i>...<b>it was fantastic</b>! Oh, wowza! I'm not sure where to begin but here goes...<br/><br/>I haven't read <i>every</i> Kristen Ashley book that's out there, but I've read more than a handful. And with every KA book I've read, I know what to expect in the hero department. He's going to be an uber-Alpha, controlling, bossy, dominant, with secrets he's reluctant to reveal, but when he eventually does, you'll see a softer, more vulner</span>
  <span id="freeText15413658050358696025" style="display:none"><i>I have to get my thoughts about this book down right now before time dilutes my feelings</i>...<b>it was fantastic</b>! Oh, wowza! I'm not sure where to begin but here goes...<br><br>I haven't read <i>every</i> Kristen Ashley book that's out there, but I've read more than a handful. And with every KA book I've read, I know what to expect in the hero department. He's going to be an uber-Alpha, controlling, bossy, dominant, with secrets he's reluctant to reveal, but when he eventually does, you'll see a softer, more vulnerable side. Oh yeah, that was Mr. Knight Sebring alright. In real life, I could never see myself with a man like Knight--despite all his good points (and there <i>were</i> many) he was just way too controlling. So how did Kristen Ashley make me fall in love with him? Ahh, that's the beauty of her writing skills! Her characters absolutely put a spell on me, and make me think with my heart instead of my head.:) <b>Knight</b> was a page-turner from the get-go, and any book that holds my attention so much that it has me forgoing sleep is a winner for me!<br><br><i>Knight...</i><br><a href="http://s880.beta.photobucket.com/user/aunteecr/media/books/ae5ddb26-38dd-4cf7-8d17-cbf0d4ba14de_zps3ea32bd1.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380374471i/728503.jpg" alt=" photo ae5ddb26-38dd-4cf7-8d17-cbf0d4ba14de_zps3ea32bd1.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The plot is simple enough. Anya Gage is a 27-year old brunette beauty, holding down multiple jobs while attending beauty school with the goal of one day owning her own fabulous spa. It may be a pipe dream, but Anya's hard-working and independent, and no one deserves a break more than Anya. She meets 35 year-old club owner Knight at a party she's reluctantly attending with her gold-digger girlfriend Sandrine. Sandrine is interested in Nick Sebring (Knight's younger brother), a notorious Denver "player", and he's got bucks and connections. While at the party and looking for a way to leave, smokin' hot Knight walks in the door, all pissed off and badass becuase there's a party going on under <i>his</i> roof. Anya and Knight cross paths when she uses the phone to call a taxi and Knight <b>insists</b> on taking her home. Anya is attracted but a little scared of Knight, but he insists she has nothing to fear from him. That's the beginning of a relationship that changes Anya's whole life, as Knight becomes more and more a part of her world (or I should say <b>she</b> becomes a part of <b>his</b> world, because that's how it is with Knight). There's smokin' hot chemistry between the two, but will Anya be okay with giving up total control to Knight? Can she do what Knight wants, live with his rules, wear what he wants her to wear, ask no questions that he isn't ready to answer and abide by decisions he makes?<br><br><i>Knight has incredibly blue eyes...</i><br><a href="http://s880.beta.photobucket.com/user/aunteecr/media/books/0371c736-79a3-4f21-b5f1-ff66dc9d45a9_zpsacec4f5a.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380374471i/728504.jpg" alt=" photo 0371c736-79a3-4f21-b5f1-ff66dc9d45a9_zpsacec4f5a.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Ms. Ashley gives us plenty of details about the characters. Anya's had a hard life since she was 7 years old, <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ when her loving parents were killed by a carjacker, and she was left with a nasty aunt who didn't care much about her. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span>Knight, hoo boy, you have to wait awhile for the big reveal about his life, but it's a stunner. It explains soooo much about him and his actions. And he is so lucky to have found Anya; it takes a special woman to understand him and accept some of the things he does, all in the name of protecting those he cares about and his world. And as more and more of his secrets were exposed, and I grew to know (and love) him, I too felt understanding when the <b>really big secret about how he makes his millions came out</b>!<br><br>The love scenes? Ummmmmmm...smokin' H-O-T...but...the use of "Daddy" as in <i>"Baby wants her Daddy" and "Daddy's gonna lick you clean"</i> doesn't always work for me. But I can deal with it with characters this hot.:) Knight was a serious dirty-talker (which <i>does</i><br>work for me) and was into a little of the kinky stuff (spanking) and some bondage, but a lot of this stuff was off the page. Fine by me. What was written was seriously <i>hawt</i>, so brace yourself.:)<br><br>And before I forget--<i>the epilogue</i>! Oh my...*swoon*...be prepared to get a little teary-eyed, is all I'll say. Just a wonderful HEA.<br><br><b>Knight</b> just may have knocked <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/11665750.At_Peace__The__Burg___2_" title="At Peace (The 'Burg, #2) by Kristen Ashley" rel="nofollow noopener">At Peace</a> off its pedestal as my favorite KA book. When you're sad because you've turned the last page and you're thinking about reading it again but this time really <i>savoring</i> it, then you know it's a winner. 5 big stars!</["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></["br"]></span>
  <a data-text-id="15413658050358696025" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

              <span id="reviewTextContainer1040714920" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer17123462092303564300"><b>5 <i>I’ll be your baby</i> Stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409585736i/10995587._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Anya, orphaned at the age of 7, is used to struggling and fighting for everything she gets. She is currently working full-time, going to school, and seeing clients on the side. She goes to a party with her friend one night and accidentally runs into Knight. <br/><br/>Knight is a successful club owner, sexy as sin, and dominating. Knight takes one look at Anya and wants to know more about her, to protect her, to own her. <br/><br/><b>
  <i>“Babe, your clothes. Shit. But you work ‘em and you do bec</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText17123462092303564300" style="display:none"><b>5 <i>I’ll be your baby</i> Stars</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409585736i/10995587._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Anya, orphaned at the age of 7, is used to struggling and fighting for everything she gets. She is currently working full-time, going to school, and seeing clients on the side. She goes to a party with her friend one night and accidentally runs into Knight. <br><br>Knight is a successful club owner, sexy as sin, and dominating. Knight takes one look at Anya and wants to know more about her, to protect her, to own her. <br><br><b>
  <i>“Babe, your clothes. Shit. But you work ‘em and you do because you’ve got one serious fantastic body, your hair is even better and your face is a face that launches a thousand hard-ons.” </i>
</b><br><br>I freaking loved Knight and his dirty talk. This is very different then KA’s other alpha’s, Knight is a little rough around the edges and may not be for everyone. I loved the “Daddy” talk and him wanting to own her. There is an instant connection between Knight and Anya, but I wouldn’t classify it has instant love. Knight wants Anya and Anya naturally wants Knight, but there isn’t any immediate <i>I love you’s</i>. There is definitely insta-lust, but HELLO this is Knight we are talking about!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409585736i/10995588._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved this story. It has the KA magic that I love, and it is probably the hottest thing I have read from her. A lot of times you get a book that is either all story or all sex, this is the perfect balance of sex and story. Anya has had a rough life and the way Knight steps in and wants to take care of her…SWOONING!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1409585736i/10995589._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I someone how missed this series, and I highly recommend it if you have somehow overlooked it too! </span>

<div id="review_460183362" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/460183362" />
    <a title="Debra" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13247178-debra"><img alt="Debra" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1473718933p2/13247178.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/460183362?book_show_action=true">Nov 20, 2012</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Debra" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Debra" href="/user/show/13247178-debra">Debra</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=alpha-male">alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=hot-hot-hot">hot-hot-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13247178-debra?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer460183362" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9937989654444174322"><br/>♦ <b>4.5 STARS.</b> ♦<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>"Your Christian name is Knight?"<br/>"If that means first name, yeah."<br/>"With a 'K'?"<br/>"Yeah, babe, with a 'K'."<br/>"That's an unusual name."<br/>"Yeah."<br/>"I kind of like it."<br/>"I can die happy."</i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>♦ <b>
  <u>KNIGHT</u>
</b> ♦<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398287i/769595._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>♦ <b>
  <u>ANYA</u>
</b> ♦<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398287i/769596._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Did you jack off, thinking of me?"<br/>"Absolutely." My womb convulsed again.<br/>I knew this sensation showed on my face because I heard him whisper, <br/>"Baby wants her Daddy."<br/>Oh.<br/>My.<br/>God.<br/>Definite mini-orgasm.<br/>"Fuck yeah, my baby wants her Daddy," he growled.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/><br/>This quote holds the reaso</span>
  <span id="freeText9937989654444174322" style="display:none"><br>♦ <b>4.5 STARS.</b> ♦<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>"Your Christian name is Knight?"<br>"If that means first name, yeah."<br>"With a 'K'?"<br>"Yeah, babe, with a 'K'."<br>"That's an unusual name."<br>"Yeah."<br>"I kind of like it."<br>"I can die happy."</i>
</blockquote><br><br>♦ <b>
  <u>KNIGHT</u>
</b> ♦<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398287i/769595._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>♦ <b>
  <u>ANYA</u>
</b> ♦<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380398287i/769596._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>"Did you jack off, thinking of me?"<br>"Absolutely." My womb convulsed again.<br>I knew this sensation showed on my face because I heard him whisper, <br>"Baby wants her Daddy."<br>Oh.<br>My.<br>God.<br>Definite mini-orgasm.<br>"Fuck yeah, my baby wants her Daddy," he growled.</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br><br>This quote holds the reason of why I was a little hesitant to read this book, and although I'm still not really a big fan of the "Daddy-calling", it somehow fitted in with the story and it didn't really bother me that much. Besides, when a man like Knight tells you to call him Daddy, you just do it, no questions asked, LOL. ;-)<br><br><p>
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398287ra/769597.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  <br>
  <br>
</p><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"You love me?"<br>"Baby, you were made for me." ❤ </i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Kinght was a fun, entertaining, HOT and at times, hilarious read with a badass alpha male and a strong, relatable heroine and I enjoyed reading every second of it!!<br><br>Why did I wait so long to read KA!? I'll definitely be reading much more of her work in the future!!<br><br><br><br><b>Full review to come. ~</b></span>
